              Form.OnShow = function() {

              Form.AddUpdate = function() {
                  var msg = '';
                  if (+getVar('LPU_GIVER_TYPE') === 2) {
                     msg = ' Не заполнено поле "ЛПУ, присвоившее льготу". Удалите или добавьте льготе ЛПУ.'
                  }
                  if (+getVar('SOPTION') === 0) {
                      if (getVar('G_CODE')) {
                          D3Api.showAlert('У пациента уже есть льгота с кодом ' + getVar('G_CODE') + msg);
                          return;
                      }
                  } else if (+getVar('SOPTION') === 2) {
                      if (getVar('MKB_CODE')) {
                          D3Api.showAlert('У пациента уже есть льгота по заболеванию ' + getVar('MKB_CODE') + msg);
                          return;
                      }
                  }
      
                  if (getValue('CONTINGENT')) {
                      executeAction('CheckContingentDateEnd', function() {
                          var warnMsg = getVar('WARN_MSG');
      
                          if (warnMsg) {
                              if (confirm(warnMsg)) {
                                  setValue('DATE_E', getVar('DATE_E_CONT'));
                              } else {
                                  return;
                              }
                          }
      
                          executeAction('CheckContingentDateBegin', function() {
                              if (getVar('WARN_MSG')) {
                                  D3Api.showAlert(getVar('WARN_MSG'));
                                  refreshDataSet('DS_CONTINGENTS');
                                  return;
                              }
      
                              Form.executeAddUpdAction();
                          });
                      });
                  } else {
                      Form.executeAddUpdAction();
                  }
              };
              Form.executeAddUpdAction = function() {
                  if (Form.isAsulon()) {
                      Form.executeAddUpdActionAsulon();
                  } else if (Form.isEfarma()) {
                      Form.executeAddUpdActionEfarma();
                  } else {
                      executeAction('ADDUPDATE_ACTION', Form.OnSuccessAddUpdate);
                  }

              Form.OnSuccessAddUpdate = function(isAsulon = false) {
                  var action = getVar('action');
      
                  if (action === 'INSERT') {
                      setVar('newid', getVar('NEW_ID'), 1);
                  }
      
                  setVar('ModalResult', 1, 1);
      
                  if (isAsulon && +getVar('IS_SNILS')) {
                      Form.callSetFlagGetRegRegistrModule();
                  } else if (Form.isEfarma() && +getVar('IS_SNILS')) {
                      var privId = getVar('action') === 'INSERT' ? getVar('NEW_ID') : getVar('ID');
                      Form.callEfarmaModule(getVar('AGENT'), privId, 'AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS', 'PersonClientSave', 'default', Form.closeAfterSuccess, Form.closeAfterError);
                  } else {
                      closeWindow();
                  }
              };

              Form._onChangeCtrlOldValues = {};
              Form.onChangeCtrl = function(_dom, _cn, _pn, _pv) {
                  // Используем не _pv, а getValue, т.к. по каким-то причинам _pv не показывает актуальное значение поля.
                  // В Form._onChangeCtrlOldValues хранятся предыдущие значения чтобы избежать лишних срабатываний,
                  // т.к. при присвоении текущего значения полю еще раз (т.е. значение не меняется), обработчик все равно вызывается
                  if (_pn !== 'value' || Form._onChangeCtrlOldValues[_cn] === getValue(_cn)) {
                      return;
                  }
      
                  Form._onChangeCtrlOldValues[_cn] = getValue(_cn);
      
                  switch(_cn) {
                      case 'PRIV_TYPE':
                          refreshDataSet('DS_CONTINGENTS');
                          var dsRow = getDataSet('DS_PRIV_TYPES').data.find(item => +item.ID === +getValue('PRIV_TYPE'));
                          dsRow && setVar('PRIV_T_CODE', dsRow['T_CODE']);
                          setVar('PRIV_TYPE_CHANGED', 1);
                          setVar('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS', getValue('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS'));
                          refreshDataSet('DS_PRIV_DIS_GROUPS');
                          break;
                      case 'PRIV_DISEASE_MKB':
                          setVar('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS', getValue('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS'));
                          refreshDataSet('DS_PRIV_DIS_GROUPS');
                          break;
                      case 'PRIV_DIS_GROUPS':
                          var val = +getValue('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS');
                          if (val) {
                              getPage().removeListener('onchangepropertyPRIV_DISEASE_MKB', Form.onChangeCtrl, Form, false);
      
                              executeAction('CheckDiseaseMkb', function() {
                                  getPage().addListener('onchangepropertyPRIV_DISEASE_MKB', Form.onChangeCtrl, Form, false);
                              });
                          }
      
                          setVar('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS', getValue('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS'));
                          Form.setDateEnd(val, 'DS_PRIV_DIS_GROUPS');
      
                          if (!Form.hasRecipe()) {
                              setEnabled('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB', !!val);
                              Form.AfterRefreshComboBoxFixEnabled('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB');
      
                              if (!val) {
                                  clearControl('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB');
                              }
                          }
      
                          break;
                  }
      
                  var pdgVal = +getValue('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS');
                  Form.MaskInspector_setRequireControl('MaskInspector', 'PRIV_DIS_GROUPS', +getValue('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB') && getValue('DATE_B') !== "");
                  Form.MaskInspector_setRequireControl('MaskInspector', 'PRIV_DISEASE_MKB', pdgVal);
              };
              Form.selectDiseaseMkb = function() {
                  var is_empty = empty(getControlProperty('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS', 'value'));
                  var data = (!is_empty) ? getControlByName('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS').selected_item.clone.data : [];
      
                  openWindow({
                      name: 'UniversalComposition/UniversalComposition',
                      unit: 'MKB10',
                      composition: 'DEFAULT',
                      vars: {
                          PRIV_GROUP_CODE: !is_empty && data['CODE'],
                          PRIV_DATE: !is_empty && getValue('DATE_B'),
                          WITH_PRIV: is_empty ? 0 : 1,
                          PRIV_DIS_GROUP_ID: !is_empty && data['ID'],
                      }
                  }, true)
                          .addListener('onafterclose', function() {
                              if (+getVar('ModalResult') === 1) {
                                  setValue('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB', getVar('return_id'));
                                  setCaption('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB', getVar('return'));
                              }
                          });
              };
              Form.afterRefresh = function(name) {
                  setValue(name, getVar(name));
      
                  if (!getValue(name)) {
                      var data = getDataSet('DS_' + name).data;
      
                      if (data.length == 1) {
                          setValue(name, data[0]['ID']);
                      }
                  }
              };
              Form.saveContingent = function() {
                  setVar('CONTINGENT', getValue('CONTINGENT'));
              };
              Form.restoreContingent = function() {
                  setValue('CONTINGENT', getVar('CONTINGENT'));
              };
              Form.validateCtrlsByDateBegin = function() {
                  var dageBegin = getValue('DATE_B');
      
                  if (dageBegin) {
                      executeAction('CheckContingentDateBegin', function() {
                          if (getVar('WARN_MSG')) {
                              D3Api.showAlert(getVar('WARN_MSG'));
                          }
                      });
                      if (dageBegin !== getVar('_DATE_B_OLD')) {
                          beginRequest();
                              refreshDataSet('DS_CONTINGENTS');
                              refreshDataSet('DS_PRIV_DIS_GROUPS');
                          endRequest();
                      }
                  }
      
                  setVar('_DATE_B_OLD', dageBegin);
              };
              //asulon

                  return +getVar('IntegrationEnabled') === 1;
              };
              Form.executeAddUpdActionAsulon = function() {
                  executeAction('getExistsSNILS', function() {
                      if (+getVar('IS_SNILS')) {
                          setVar('STATUS', 3);

                      } else {
                          D3Api.showConfirm('Необходимо заполнить СНИЛС пациента и сохранить карту.', function() {
                              setVar('STATUS', 2);
                              executeAction('ADDUPDATE_ACTION', function() {
                                  Form.OnSuccessAddUpdate(true);
                              });
                          }, null, {
                              button_confirm_caption: 'Сохранить все равно',
                              button_cancel_caption: 'Отмена'
                          });
                      }
                  });
              };
              Form.executeAddUpdActionEfarma = function() {
                  executeAction('getExistsSNILS', function() {
                      if (+getVar('IS_SNILS')) {
                          executeAction('ADDUPDATE_ACTION', Form.OnSuccessAddUpdate);
                      } else {
                          D3Api.showConfirm('Необходимо заполнить СНИЛС пациента и сохранить карту.');
                      }
                  });
              };
              Form.callSetFlagGetRegRegistrModule = function(){
                  function onSuccessExec(){
                      executeAction('ADD_PRIV_SAULON_LINK');
      
                      if (+getVar('result') !== 0) {
                          closeWindow();
                      } else {
                          D3Api.showAlert(getVar('error'), 'Ошибка', null, null, closeWindow);
                      }
                  }
      
                  function onErrorExec() {
                      D3Api.showAlert('Ошибка работы модуля', null)
                  }
      
                  executeModule('SetFlagGetRegRegistr', onSuccessExec, onErrorExec);
              };
              Form.onPrivTypeChange = function() {
                  var privTypeId = +getValue('PRIV_TYPE');
                  var isOrph = !!(Form.privTypes[privTypeId] && Form.privTypes[privTypeId].code === 6);
      
                  // если выбран тип льготы - орфанные заболевания, сделать поле CODE_UNRZ_STR активным и обязательным
                  MaskInspector_setRequireControl('MaskInspector', 'CODE_UNRZ_STR', isOrph);
                  setEnabled('CODE_UNRZ_STR', isOrph);
                  // Иначе - очищаем
                  if (!isOrph) {
                      setValue('CODE_UNRZ_STR', null);
                  }
              };
              Form.onChangePriv = function(name) {
                  var ctrlArr;
      
                  if (name === 'PRIV_DISEASE_MKB') {
                      ctrlArr = ['CONTINGENT', 'PRIV_DISEASE_MKB'];
                  } else {
                      ctrlArr = ['PRIV_DIS_GROUPS', 'PRIV_DISEASE_MKB']
                  }
      
                  ctrlArr.forEach(function(item) {
                      if (getValue(item)) {
                          setValue(item, '');
                          setCaption(item, '');
                          setVar(item, null);
                      }
                  });
              };
              Form.onChangePrivType = function() {
                  if (getValue('PRIV_TYPE') !== +getVar('PRIV_TYPE')) {
                      ['CONTINGENT', 'PRIV_DIS_GROUPS', 'PRIV_DISEASE_MKB'].forEach(function(item) {
                          if (getValue(item)) {
                              setValue(item, '');
                              setCaption(item, '');
                              setVar(item, null);
                          }
                      });
      
                      setEnabled('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB', false);
      
                      if (+getVar('PRIV_TYPE')) {
                          if (Form.hasInDsRow('DS_PRIV_TYPES', getVar('PRIV_TYPE'), 'T_CODE', 8)) {
                              setValue('DATE_E', '');
                          }
                      }
                  }
      
                  setVar('PRIV_TYPE', getValue('PRIV_TYPE'));
              };
              Form.onChangePrivContingent = function() {
                  var contingent = +getValue('CONTINGENT');
                  var contingateDate = null;
                  var changeContingateDate = !getVar('onLoadContingent');
      
                  if (!contingent) {
                      return;
                  }
      
                  switch (contingent) {
                      case +getVar('privChildThreeYearId'):
                          contingateDate = Form.getDateEndByAgentBirthdate(3);
                          setVar('contingetnDateEnd', contingateDate);
                          changeContingateDate && setValue('DATE_E', contingateDate);
                          break;
                      case +getVar('privLargeFamilyChildId'):
                          contingateDate = Form.getDateEndByAgentBirthdate(6);
                          changeContingateDate && setValue('DATE_E', contingateDate);
                          break;
                      default:
                          Form.setDateEnd(getValue('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS'), 'DS_PRIV_DIS_GROUPS');
                          break;
                  }
      
                  setVar('onLoadContingent', '');
              };

                  Form.checkBeforeOnButtonOk = function(callback) {
                      if (typeof(Form.CheckSnils) === 'function' && !Form.CheckSnils()) {
                          return;
                      }
      
                      if (!getValue('CONTINGENT') && !getValue('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB')) {
                          D3Api.showAlert('Ошибка в региональной льготе: Заполните либо льготный контингент, либо льготное заболевание!');
                          return;

                      callback && callback();
                  };
      
                  Form.checkBeforeOnButtonOkAsulon = function(callback) {
                      if ((getValue('DATE_B') || getValue('DATE_E')) && getVar("action") == "UPDATE") {
                          executeAction('checkEndDate', null, null, 0, 0);
      
                          if (getVar('MIN_REC_DATE') || getVar('MAX_REC_DATE')) {
                              D3Api.showAlert('Найдены рецепты вне периода действия льготы: '+getVar('MIN_REC_DATE')+' - '+getVar('MAX_REC_DATE')+'. Льгота должна действовать в этот период.');
                              return;
                          }
                      }
      
                      if (!getValue('DATE_E') && getVar("action") === "UPDATE") {
                          executeAction('getCurLpuDict', null, null, 0, 0);
      
                          if (getVar('LPU_GIVER') && getVar('CUR_LPUDICT') !== getVar('LPU_GIVER')) {
                              D3Api.showAlert('Вы редактируете льготу, внесенную в '+getVar('LPU_GIVER_CODE')+'. '+
                                  'Чтобы добавить льготу в '+getVar('CUR_LPUDICT_CODE')+', необходимо сначала закрыть действующую льготу, укажите дату в поле «Дата снятия с льготы»');
                              return;
                          }
                      }
      
                      if (typeof(Form.CheckSnils) === 'function') {
                          if(!Form.CheckSnils()) {
                              return;
                          }
                      }
      
                      if (!getValue('CONTINGENT') && !getValue('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB')) {
                          D3Api.showAlert('Ошибка в региональной льготе: Заполните либо льготный контингент, либо льготное заболевание!');
                          return;
                      }
      
                      if (getValue('PRIV_TYPE')) {
                          if (getValue('CONTINGENT')) {
                              executeAction('checkContingentPriv', function(){
                                  if (getVar('IS_RIGHT_CONT_PRIV') !== '1') {
                                      D3Api.showAlert('Тип льготы не соответствует льготному контингенту');
                                      return;
                                  } else {
                                      callback && callback();
                                  }
                              });
                          } else {
                              callback && callback();
                          }
                      } else {
                          callback && callback();
                      }
                  };
                  Form.checkBeforeOnButtonOkEfarma = function(callback) {
                      Form.checkBeforeOnButtonOk(callback);
                  };
                  Form.OnButtonOk = function() {
                      function checkBeforeOnButtonOk() {
                          var _callback = function() {
                              executeAction('checkAgentSszRegionalPriv', function() {
                                  setVar('actionF',getVar('action'));
                                  setVar('action', 'GET_ERRORS');
                                  executeAction('ADDUPDATE_ACTION', Form.AfterCheck);
                              });
                          };
      
                          executeAction('GetGCode', function() {
                              if (Form.isAsulon()) {
                                  Form.checkBeforeOnButtonOkAsulon(_callback);
                              } else if (Form.isEfarma()) {
                                  Form.checkBeforeOnButtonOkEfarma(_callback);
                              } else {
                                  Form.checkBeforeOnButtonOk(_callback);
                              }
                          });
                      };
      
                      if (!Form.checkDateEnd()) {
                          return;
                      }
      
                      if (getValue('MKB_DATE') && !getDateCompare(getValue('MKB_DATE'), getVar('SYSDATE'))) {
                          D3Api.showAlert('Дата установки диагноза не может быть больше текущей даты');
                          return;
                      }
      
                      if (!getDateCompare(getValue('DATE_B'), getVar('SYSDATE'))) {
                          D3Api.showAlert('Дата начала действия льготы не может быть больше текущей даты');
                          return;
                      }
      
                      if (Form.hasRecipe() && !getDateCompare(getVar('RECIPE_REC_DATE'), getValue('DATE_E'))) {
                          setValue('DATE_E', null);
                          D3Api.showAlert('Дата окончания должна быть больше или равна дате рецепта: ' + getVar('RECIPE_REC_DATE'));
                          return;
                      }
      
                      if ([+getVar('privChildThreeYearId'), +getVar('privLargeFamilyChildId')].includes(+getValue('CONTINGENT'))) {
                          executeAction('checkPrivSo', function() {
                              if (+getVar('isPrivSo')) {
                                  let code = +getValue('CONTINGENT') === +getVar('privChildThreeYearId') ? getVar('privLargeFamilyChilCode') : getVar('privChildThreeYearCode');
                                  D3Api.showAlert('У пациента имеется действующая льгота с кодом ' + code + '. Добавление невозможно.');
                                  return;
                              } else {
                                  checkBeforeOnButtonOk();
                              }
                          })
                      } else {
                          checkBeforeOnButtonOk();
                      }
                  };
                  Form.onBlurDiseaseMkb_oldCaption = null;
                  Form.onBlurDiseaseMkb = function() {
                      if (Form.onBlurDiseaseMkb_oldCaption !== getCaption('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB')) {
                          ButtonEdit_Validate(getControlByName('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB'));
                      }
      
                      Form.onBlurDiseaseMkb_oldCaption = getCaption('PRIV_DISEASE_MKB');
                  };
                  Form.onChangeDateB = function(onBlur = false) {
                      if (!onBlur || getEnabled('DATE_B')) {
                          Form.validateCtrlsByDateBegin();
                          Form.setDateEnd(getValue('PRIV_DIS_GROUPS'), 'DS_PRIV_DIS_GROUPS');
                      }
                  };
              

СИСТЕМНЫЕ ОПЦИИ:
  - CodesMoForPrivs
  - PrivCodeChildThreeYear
  - PrivCodeLargeFamilyChild
  - PrivCodeMyocardialInfarction
  - RegistrSszGroupCodes

  [4] M2 Action: checkAgentRegPrivUniqueMKB
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/Agents/agent_regional_privs/regional_priv_edit.frm
      SQL:
      
              declare
                nARP_ID                 D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS_BASE.ID%type;
                rARP                    D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS_BASE%rowtype;
                nIS_LPU_GIVER           NUMBER(1) := 0;
              begin
                  :SOPTION := D_PKG_OPTION_SPECS.GET('AgentRegPrivUniqueMKB', :pnLPU);
                  if :saction = 'INSERT' then
                      if :IntegrationEnabled = 1 and :pnLPU_GIVER is not null then
                        select count(1)
                          into nIS_LPU_GIVER
                          from dual t
                         where :pnLPU_GIVER_CODE in (select /*+ cardinality(t,1)*/ t.COLUMN_VALUE
                                                       from table(cast(D_PKG_TOOLS.STR_SEPARATE(D_PKG_OPTIONS.GET('CodesMoForPrivs', :pnLPU, 0), ';') as D_CL_STR)) t);
                      end if;
      
                      if :SOPTION in (0, 1) then
                        begin
                          select max(arp.PRIV_GROUP),
                               @if (:IntegrationEnabled == 1) {
                                 max(case when arp.LPU_GIVER_ID is null and nIS_LPU_GIVER = 1 then 2 else 1 end)
                               @} else {
                                 1
                               @}
                            into :G_CODE,
                                 :LPU_GIVER_TYPE
                            from D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS arp
                           where arp.PID = :pnAGENT
                             and arp.PRIV_GROUP_ID = :pnPRIV_GROUP
                             and (arp.DATE_E is null or
                                 (arp.DATE_B <= :pdDATE_B and :pdDATE_B <= arp.DATE_E))
                             and arp.PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID = :pnPRIV_DISEASE_MKB
                           @if (:IntegrationEnabled == 1) {
                             and (nIS_LPU_GIVER = 0 or coalesce(arp.LPU_GIVER_ID, to_number(:pnLPU_GIVER)) = to_number(:pnLPU_GIVER));
                           @} else {
                             and rownum = 1;
                           @}
                        exception when no_data_found then
                          :G_CODE := null;
                        end;
                      elsif :SOPTION = 2 then
                        begin
                          select max(arp.PRIV_DISEASE_MKB),
                               @if (:IntegrationEnabled == 1) {
                                 max(case when arp.LPU_GIVER_ID is null and nIS_LPU_GIVER = 1 then 2 else 1 end)
                               @} else {
                                 1
                               @}
                            into :MKB_CODE,
                                 :LPU_GIVER_TYPE
                            from D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS arp
                           where arp.PID = :pnAGENT
                             and (arp.DATE_E is null or
                                 (arp.DATE_B <= :pdDATE_B and :pdDATE_B <= arp.DATE_E))
                             and arp.PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID = :pnPRIV_DISEASE_MKB
                           @if (:IntegrationEnabled == 1) {
                             and (nIS_LPU_GIVER = 0 or coalesce(arp.LPU_GIVER_ID, to_number(:pnLPU_GIVER)) = to_number(:pnLPU_GIVER));
                           @} else {
                             and rownum = 1;
                           @}
                        exception when no_data_found then
                          :MKB_CODE := null;
                        end;
                      end if;
      
                      begin
                        select arp.ID
                          into nARP_ID
                          from D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS_BASE arp
                         where arp.ID = :pnAGENT
                           and arp.PRIV_GROUP_ID != :pnPRIV_GROUP
                           and (arp.DATE_E is null or
                               (arp.DATE_B <= :pdDATE_B and :pdDATE_B <= arp.DATE_E))
                           and arp.PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID = :pnPRIV_DISEASE_MKB
                           and rownum = 1;
                      exception when no_data_found then
                        nARP_ID := null;
                      end;
                  end if;
      
                  if :SOPTION = 1 then
                      if :G_CODE is not null then
                        D_P_EXC('У пациента уже есть льгота с кодом ' || :G_CODE);
                      elsif nARP_ID is not null then
                        select *
                          into rARP
                          from D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS_BASE t
                         where t.ID = nARP_ID;
      
                        D_PKG_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.UPD(nARP_ID,
                                                       :PNLPU,
                                                       rARP.CONTINGENT_ID,
                                                       rARP.PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID,
                                                       rARP.STATUS,
                                                       rARP.DATE_B,
                                                       to_date(:pdDATE_B, 'DD.MM.YYYY') - 1,
                                                       rARP.PRIVDOC_KIND_ID,
                                                       rARP.PRIVDOC_SER,
                                                       rARP.PRIVDOC_NUMB,
                                                       rARP.PRIVDOC_DATE,
                                                       rARP.LPU_GIVER_ID,
                                                       rARP.PRIV_GROUP_ID);
                      end if;
                  end if;
      
                  if nARP_ID is not null then
                    :action := 'INSERT';
                  else
                    :action := :saction;
                  end if;
              end;

              declare
                nVERSION_CONTINGENTS    NUMBER(17) := D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'CONTINGENTS');
              begin
                :PRIV_CODE_CHILD_THREE_YEAR := trim(D_PKG_OPTIONS.GET('PrivCodeChildThreeYear', :LPU, 0));

                    from D_V_CONTINGENTS_BASE t
                   where t.CODE = :PRIV_CODE_LARGE_FAMILY_CHILD
                     and t.VERSION = nVERSION_CONTINGENTS
                     and rownum = 1;
                exception when no_data_found then
                  :PRIV_LARGE_FAMILY_CHILD_ID := null;
                end;
      
                select trunc(a.BIRTHDATE)
                  into :AGENT_BIRTHDATE
                  from D_V_AGENTS_BASE a
                 where a.ID = :AGENT_ID;
              end;

  [9] M2 Action: ADDUPDATE_ACTION
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/Agents/agent_regional_privs/regional_priv_edit.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare
                    rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS   D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS_BASE%rowtype;
                    nPERIOD                 NUMBER(4);
                    nUSER_ID                NUMBER(17);
                    nFLAG                   NUMBER(1) := 0;
                  begin
                    if :AgentTargetProgram = '1' and :action <> 'GET_ERRORS' then
                      select t.*
                        into rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS
                        from D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS_BASE t
                       where t.ID = coalesce(:NEWID, :ID);
      
                      select t.SYSUSER
                        into nUSER_ID
                        from D_V_EMPLOYERS_BASE t
                       where t.ID = :EMPLOYER;
      
                      if :pdDATE_E is not null then
                        rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.SYSUSER_ENDED := nUSER_ID;
                        rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.DATE_END_IS_AUTO := 0;
                        nFLAG := 1;
                      end if;
      
                      if :pnTARGET_PROGRAM is not null and :pdDATE_E is null then
                        select t.PERIOD
                          into nPERIOD
                          from D_V_TARGET_PROGRAM_BASE t
                         where t.ID = :pnTARGET_PROGRAM;
      
                        if nPERIOD is not null then
                          rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.DATE_E := rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.DATE_B + nPERIOD;
                          rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.SYSUSER_ENDED := nUSER_ID;
                          rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.DATE_END_IS_AUTO := 0;
                          nFLAG := 1;
                        end if;
                      elsif :pnTARGET_PROGRAM is null and :action = 'UPDATE' then
                        rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.TARGET_PROGRAM_ID := null;
                        nFLAG := 1;
                      end if;
                      if nFLAG = 1 then
                        D_PKG_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.UPD(pnID               => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.ID,
                                                       pnLPU              => :LPU,
                                                       pnCONTINGENT       => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.CONTINGENT_ID,
                                                       pnPRIV_DISEASE_MKB => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID,
                                                       pnSTATUS           => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.STATUS,
                                                       pdDATE_B           => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.DATE_B,
                                                       pdDATE_E           => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.DATE_E,
                                                       pnPRIVDOC_KIND     => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.PRIVDOC_KIND_ID,
                                                       psPRIVDOC_SER      => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.PRIVDOC_SER,
                                                       psPRIVDOC_NUMB     => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.PRIVDOC_NUMB,
                                                       pdPRIVDOC_DATE     => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.PRIVDOC_DATE,
                                                       pnLPU_GIVER        => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.LPU_GIVER_ID,
                                                       pnPRIV_GROUP       => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.PRIV_GROUP_ID,
                                                       pnCODE_UNRZ        => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.CODE_UNRZ,
                                                       pnCODE_UNRZ_STR    => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.CODE_UNRZ_STR,
                                                       vAPI_VERSION       => 4,
                                                       pdMKB_DATE         => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.MKB_DATE,
                                                       pnTARGET_PROGRAM   => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.TARGET_PROGRAM_ID,
                                                       pnSYSUSER_ENDED    => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.SYSUSER_ENDED,
                                                       pnDATE_END_IS_AUTO => rAGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS.DATE_END_IS_AUTO);
                      end if;
                    end if;
                  exception when others then
                    D_P_EXC(SQLERRM);
                  end;

  [11] M2 Action: SelectAction
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/Agents/agent_regional_privs/regional_priv_edit.frm
      SQL:
      
              begin
                  select t.PID,
                         t.CONTINGENT_ID,
                         t.CONTINGENT,
                         t.PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID,
                         t.PRIV_DISEASE_MKB,
                         t.DATE_B,
                         t.DATE_E,
                         t.PRIVDOC_KIND_ID,
                         t.PRIVDOC_SER,
                         t.PRIVDOC_NUMB,
                         t.PRIVDOC_DATE,
                         t.STATUS,
                         t.LPU_GIVER_ID,
                         (select s.PRIV_TYPE_ID
                            from D_V_PRIV_DIS_GROUPS s
                           where s.ID = t.PRIV_GROUP_ID),
                         (select s.PRIV_TYPE_ID
                            from D_V_CONTINGENTS s
                           where s.ID = t.CONTINGENT_ID),
                         t.PRIV_GROUP_ID,
                         t.MKB_DATE,
                         t.TARGET_PROGRAM_ID,
                         t.TARGET_PROGRAM_NAME,
                         case when :IntegrationEnabled = 1 then t.CODE_UNRZ_STR end,
                         D_PKG_UNITPROPS.GET_SVAL('AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS', t.ID, 'REG_NUM_P', 0)
                    into :PID,
                         :CONTINGENT_ID,
                         :CONTINGENT,
                         :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID,
                         :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB,
                         :DATE_B,
                         :DATE_E,
                         :PRIVDOC_KIND,
                         :PRIVDOC_SER,
                         :PRIVDOC_NUMB,
                         :PRIVDOC_DATE,
                         :STATUS,
                         :LPU_GIVER,
                         :PRIV_TYPE_MKB,
                         :PRIV_TYPE_CONT,
                         :PRIV_GROUP_ID,
                         :MKB_DATE,
                         :TARGET_PROGRAM,
                         :TARGET_PROGRAM_NAME,
                         :CODE_UNRZ_STR,
                         :REG_NUM_P
                    from D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS t
                   where t.ID = :ID;
      
                  select trunc(max(r.REC_DATE))
                    into :RECIPE_REC_DATE
                    from D_V_RECIPS r
                   where r.PAT_AGENT = :PID
                     and r.LPU = :LPU
                     and (r.REG_CONTINGENT_ID = :CONTINGENT_ID
                          or (r.REG_DISEASE_ID = :PRIV_GROUP_ID
                              and r.DISEASE_ID = :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID));
      
                  :HAS_RECIPE := case when :RECIPE_REC_DATE is not null then 1 else 0 end;
              end;

  [14] M2 DataSet: DS_PRIV_DIS_GROUPS
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/Agents/agent_regional_privs/regional_priv_edit.frm
      SQL:
      
              select t.ID,
                     t.G_CODE CODE,
                     t.G_CODE||' '||t.G_NAME NAME
                from D_V_PRIV_DIS_GROUPS t
                     join D_V_PRIV_DIS_DIAPASONES pdd on pdd.PID = t.ID
               where t.VERSION = (select D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'PRIV_DIS_GROUPS') from dual)
                 and (pdd.DATE_B <= :DATE_B and (pdd.DATE_E >= :DATE_B or pdd.DATE_E is null))
               @if (:PRIV_TYPE) {
                 and t.PRIV_TYPE_ID = :PRIV_TYPE
               @}
               @if (:PRIV_DISEASE_MKB) {
                 and D_PKG_MKB10.CHECK_RANGE((select mkb.MKB_CODE
                                                from D_V_MKB10_BASE mkb
                                               where mkb.ID = :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB), pdd.MKB_CODE_B, pdd.MKB_CODE_E) = 1
               @}
               group by t.ID, t.G_CODE, t.G_CODE || ' ' || t.G_NAME
               order by t.G_CODE, t.G_CODE || ' ' || t.G_NAME, ID

  [15] M2 Action: CheckDiseaseMkb
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/Agents/agent_regional_privs/regional_priv_edit.frm
      SQL:
      
              declare
                nCOUNT                 NUMBER(17);
              begin
                select count(1)
                  into nCOUNT
                  from D_V_PRIV_DIS_DIAPASONES pdd
                 where pdd.VERSION = (select D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'PRIV_DIS_DIAPASONES')
                                        from dual)
                   and pdd.PID = :PRIV_DIS_GROUPS
                   and pdd.DATE_B <= :DATE_B
                   and (pdd.DATE_E >= :DATE_B or pdd.DATE_E is null);
      
                if nCOUNT != 1 then
                  :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID := :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_OLD;
                  :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB := :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_CAPTION_OLD;
                  return;
                end if;
      
                select t.ID,
                       t.MKB_CODE
                  into :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID,
                       :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB
                  from D_V_MKB10 t
                 where t.VERSION = (select D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'MKB10')
                                      from dual)
                   and t.ID = :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_OLD
                   and exists(select null
                                from D_V_PRIV_DIS_DIAPASONES pdd
                               where pdd.VERSION = (select D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'PRIV_DIS_DIAPASONES')
                                                      from dual)
                                 and pdd.PID = :PRIV_DIS_GROUPS
                                 and t.MKB_CODE between pdd.MKB_CODE_B and pdd.MKB_CODE_E
                                 and (pdd.DATE_B <= :DATE_B and (pdd.DATE_E >= :DATE_B or pdd.DATE_E is null)));
              exception when no_data_found then
                begin
                  select m.ID,
                         m.MKB_CODE
                    into :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID,
                         :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB
                    from D_V_PRIV_DIS_DIAPASONES pdd
                         join D_V_MKB10 m on m.ID = pdd.MKB_B
                                         and pdd.MKB_B = pdd.MKB_E
                   where pdd.VERSION = (select D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'PRIV_DIS_DIAPASONES')
                                          from dual)
                     and (pdd.DATE_B <= :DATE_B and (pdd.DATE_E >= :DATE_B or pdd.DATE_E is null))
                     and pdd.PID = :PRIV_DIS_GROUPS;
                exception when others then
                  if :PRIV_T_CODE = 4 and :PRIV_TYPE_CHANGED = 1 then
                    :PRIV_TYPE_CHANGED := 0;
                    begin
                      select m.ID,
                             m.MKB_CODE
                        into :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID,
                             :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB
                        from D_V_MKB10 m
                       where m.VERSION = (select D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'MKB10')
                                            from dual)
                         and m.MKB_CODE = (select D_PKG_CONSTANTS.SEARCH_STR('PALLIATIVE_MKB', :LPU)
                                             from dual);
                    exception when no_data_found then
                      :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID := null;
                      :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB := null;
                    end;
                  else
                    :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB_ID := null;
                    :PRIV_DISEASE_MKB := null;
                  end if;
                end;
              end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_PRIV_DIS_DIAPASONES;
          D_V_MKB10;

  [21] M2 ModuleVar: result
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/Agents/agent_regional_privs/regional_priv_edit.frm
      SQL:
      
              begin
                select to_char(min(r.REC_DATE), 'DD.MM.YYYY'),
                       to_char(max(r.REC_DATE), 'DD.MM.YYYY') --даты передавать в сообщение об ошибке
                  into :MIN_REC_DATE,
                       :MAX_REC_DATE
                  from D_V_RECIPS r
                 where r.PAT_AGENT = :PID
                   and (r.REG_DISEASE_ID = :PRIV_GROUP_ID or r.REG_CONTINGENT_ID = :CONTINGENT_ID)
                   and r.IS_REVOKED = 0 and r.IS_DELETE = 0 --рецепт не аннулирован и не удален
                   and ((trunc(r.REC_DATE) < to_date(:DATE_B) or trunc(r.REC_DATE) > nvl(to_date(:DATE_E), sysdate))) --значения дат, которые передаются при редактировании записи льготы
                   -- на дату выписки рецепта в данном ЛПУ не существует рег.льгот в истории льгот, проверяем все льготы добавленные в том же ЛПУ, что и выписанный рецепт:
                   and not exists (select null
                                     from D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS arp
                                          join D_V_LPU l on l.LPUDICT_ID = arp.LPU_GIVER_ID
                                    where l.ID = r.LPU
                                      and arp.PID = r.PAT_AGENT
                                      and (arp.PRIV_GROUP = r.REG_DISEASE or arp.CONTINGENT_ID = r.REG_CONTINGENT_ID)
                                      and ((trunc(r.REC_DATE) >= trunc(arp.DATE_B) and (trunc(r.REC_DATE) <= trunc(arp.DATE_E) or arp.DATE_E is null) and arp.ID != :ID)) --исключаем редактируемую запись льготы
                                 );
              exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                :MIN_REC_DATE := null;
                :MAX_REC_DATE := null;
              end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_LPU;
          D_V_AGENT_REGIONAL_PRIVS;
          D_V_RECIPS;

  [2] M2 Action: getSocStateConst
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/Agents/agent_social_states/agent_social_states_edit.frm
      SQL:
      
              declare
                nSOC_CATEGORY NUMBER(1);
              begin
                if :SOCST_CODE_CONST is not null then
                  begin
                    select case when ass.SOCIAL_STATE = :SOCST_CODE_CONST
                                  then ass.SOCIAL_CATEGORY
                                else ass.SOCIAL_SOCIAL_CATEGORY
                           end SOCIAL_CATEGORY
                      into nSOC_CATEGORY
                      from D_V_AGENT_SOCIAL_STATES ass
                     where ass.SOCIAL_STATE_ID = :SOCIALSTATE_ID
                       and ass.PID = :AGENT
                       and (ass.BEGIN_DATE <= trunc(sysdate)
                            and (ass.END_DATE >= trunc(sysdate) or ass.END_DATE is null));
                  exception when no_data_found then
                    nSOC_CATEGORY := null;
                  end;
                end if;
      
                if :SOCIALSTATE_ID is not null and nSOC_CATEGORY is null then
                  begin
                    select t.SOCIAL_CATEGORY,
                           t.IS_ACTIVE
                      into nSOC_CATEGORY,
                           :IS_ACTIVE
                      from D_V_SOCIALSTATES t
                     where t.ID = :SOCIALSTATE_ID;
                  exception when no_data_found then
                    nSOC_CATEGORY := 1;
                    :IS_ACTIVE := null;
                  end;
                end if;
      
                :SOCIAL_CATEGORY := nSOC_CATEGORY;
              end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_AGENT_SOCIAL_STATES;
          D_V_SOCIALSTATES;

  [7] M2 Action: GetParamFromOption
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/Agents/agent_social_states/agent_social_states_edit.frm
      SQL:
      begin
      			:RESULT := D_PKG_OPTION_SPECS.GET(:OPTION, :LPU);
      			IF :RESULT = 1 THEN
      				IF :DATE_IN is not null
      					THEN :DATE   := trunc(to_date(:DATE_IN, 'DD.MM.YYYY') - 1);
      					ELSE :DATE   := null;
      				END IF;
      				SELECT count (1)
      					INTO :COUNT
      				FROM d_v_agent_social_states t
      				WHERE t.PID  = :PID;
      				IF :COUNT = 0
      					THEN :RESULT := 0;
      				END IF;
      			END IF;
      		end;

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_AGENT_SOCIAL_STATES;

              declare
                nC_KIND            NUMBER;
                nPLACE_DEATH_ID    NUMBER;
              begin
                select D_PKG_CERTIFICATE_FORMS.GET_C_NUM(cf.C_NUM) C_NUM_CHAR,
                     to_char(cf.DATE_OUT, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D),
                     (select dt.ID
                        from D_V_DOC_TYPES dt
                       where dt.DT_CODE = D_PKG_CONSTANTS.SEARCH_STR(case when cf.C_KIND = 2
                                                                            then 'DOC_TYPE_DEATH'
                                                                          else 'DOC_TYPE_PERDEATH'
                                                                     end, :LPU, t.DATE_DEATH, 0)
                         and dt.VERSION = D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'DOC_TYPES')
                     ),
                     cf.C_KIND,
                     t.PLACE_DEATH_ID
                into :DEATHDOCNUM,
                     :DEATHDOCDATE,
                     :DEATHDOCTYPE,
                     nC_KIND,
                     nPLACE_DEATH_ID
                from D_V_CERTIFICATE_FORMS_BASE cf
                     join (select pc.DATE_DEATH,
                                  DATE_BIRTH,
                                  pc.PID,
                                  pc.AGENT_ID,
                                  pc.STATUS,
                                  pc.PLACE_DEATH_ID
                             from D_V_CF_PERDEATH_CONTENTS pc
                            where LPU = :LPU
                         union all
                           select dc.DATE_DEATH,
                                  null,
                                  dc.PID,
                                  dc.AGENT_ID,
                                  dc.STATUS,
                                  dc.PLACE_DEATH_ID
                             from D_V_CF_DEATH_CONTENTS    dc
                            where LPU = :LPU
                          ) t on t.PID = cf.ID
               where cf.LPU = :LPU
                 and cf.ID = :CF_ID;
      
                if nC_KIND = 2 and nPLACE_DEATH_ID is not null then
                  begin
                    select g.GEOLOCTYPE || '. ' || g.GEONAME
                      into :DEATHPLACE
                      from D_V_GEOGRAFY g
                     where g.TYPE = 1
                   connect by g.ID = prior g.PID
                     start with g.ID = nPLACE_DEATH_ID;
                    exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                      :DEATHPLACE := '';
                  end;
                  begin
                    select :DEATHPLACE || ', ' || g.GEOLOCTYPE || '. ' || g.GEONAME
                      into :DEATHPLACE
                      from D_V_GEOGRAFY g
                     where g.TYPE = 2
                   connect by g.ID = prior g.PID
                     start with g.ID = nPLACE_DEATH_ID;
                   exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                     :DEATHPLACE := :DEATHPLACE;
                  end;
                  begin
                    select :DEATHPLACE || ', ' || g.GEOLOCTYPE || '. ' || g.GEONAME
                      into :DEATHPLACE
                      from D_V_GEOGRAFY g
                     where g.TYPE = 3
                   connect by g.ID = prior g.PID
                     start with g.ID = nPLACE_DEATH_ID;
                   exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                     :DEATHPLACE := :DEATHPLACE;
                  end;
                  begin
                    select :DEATHPLACE || ', ' || g.GEOLOCTYPE || '. ' || g.GEONAME
                      into :DEATHPLACE
                      from D_V_GEOGRAFY g
                     where g.TYPE = 4
                   connect by g.ID = prior g.PID
                     start with g.ID = nPLACE_DEATH_ID;
                   exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                     :DEATHPLACE := :DEATHPLACE;
                  end;
                  begin
                    select :DEATHPLACE || ', ' || g.GEOLOCTYPE || '. ' || g.GEONAME
                      into :DEATHPLACE
                      from D_V_GEOGRAFY g
                     where g.TYPE = 5
                   connect by g.ID = prior g.PID
                     start with g.ID = nPLACE_DEATH_ID;
                   exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                     :DEATHPLACE := :DEATHPLACE;
                  end;
                  begin
                    select :DEATHPLACE || decode(dc.PL_DEATH_HOUSE, null, '', ', д. ' || dc.PL_DEATH_HOUSE) || decode(dc.PL_DEATH_FLAT, null, '', ', кв. ' || dc.PL_DEATH_FLAT)
                      into :DEATHPLACE
                      from D_V_CF_DEATH_CONTENTS dc
                     where dc.PID = :CF_ID;
                    exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                      :DEATHPLACE := :DEATHPLACE;
                  end;
                end if;
      
                if nC_KIND = 3 and nPLACE_DEATH_ID is not null then
                  begin
                    select g.GEOLOCTYPE || '. ' || g.GEONAME
                      into :DEATHPLACE
                      from D_V_GEOGRAFY g
                     where g.TYPE = 1
                   connect by g.ID = prior g.PID
                     start with g.ID = nPLACE_DEATH_ID;
                   exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                     :DEATHPLACE := '';
                  end;
                  begin
                    select :DEATHPLACE || ', ' || g.GEOLOCTYPE || '. ' || g.GEONAME
                      into :DEATHPLACE
                      from D_V_GEOGRAFY g
                     where g.TYPE = 2
                   connect by g.ID = prior g.PID
                     start with g.ID = nPLACE_DEATH_ID;
                   exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                     :DEATHPLACE := :DEATHPLACE;
                  end;
                  begin
                    select :DEATHPLACE || ', ' || g.GEOLOCTYPE || '. ' || g.GEONAME
                      into :DEATHPLACE
                      from D_V_GEOGRAFY g
                     where g.TYPE in (3, 4)
                   connect by g.ID = prior g.PID
                     start with g.ID = nPLACE_DEATH_ID;
                   exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                     :DEATHPLACE := :DEATHPLACE;
                  end;
                end if;
                  exception when no_data_found then
                    :DEATHDOCNUM := null;
                    :DEATHDOCDATE := null;
                    :DEATHDOCTYPE := null;
                    :DEATHPLACE := null;
              end;

              Form.findMinTime = function(arr) {
                  arr.sort((a, b) => {
                      const timeA = a.data.TIME_TEXT;
                      const timeB = b.data.TIME_TEXT;
                      return timeA.localeCompare(timeB);
                  });
      
                  return arr[0].data.TIME_TEXT;
              }
      
              Form.checkActiveDuration = function() {
                  if (!empty(getValue('DURATION'))) {
                      CheckBox_SetChecked(getControlByName('DURING'), true);
                      Edit_SetEnabled(getControlByName('DURATION'), true);
                      ComboBox_SetEnabled(getControlByName('MEASURE'), true);
                  }
              }
      
              Form.hideNotMnn = function() {
                  // Убираем надпись под Препаратом
                  setCaption('NOMMODIF_NAME', '');
                  ['dosageForm',
                      'cmbDoseMeasure',
                      'ACM_DOSE'].forEach(function(name) {
                      setDomVisible(getControlByName(name), true);
                  });
                  refreshDataSet('dsMedForms');
                  refreshDataSet('dsDoseMeasures');
                  setValue('cmbMedForms', getVar('cmbMedFormsVar'));
                  ['cmbMedForms',
                      'cmbDoseMeasure'].forEach(function(name) {
                      MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', name);
                  });
                  ['NOMMODIF',
                      'ALT_MEASURE_DOSE',

                      'ALT_MEASURE_CODE',
                      'QUANTITY',
                      'QUANTITY_L'
                  ].forEach(function(name) {

                  });
              }

                              }
      
                              setVar('DOSE', getValue('DOSE'));
                              setVar('QUANTITY', getValue('QUANTITY'));
                              Form.onChangeQuantity();
                          });
                      });
      
                      getControlByName('COMMENTARY').style.display = '';
                      getControlByName('COMM_LABEL').style.display = '';
                      setCaption('OkButton', 'Назначить и продолжить');
                      setWindowCaption('Лекарственные назначения: копирование');
      
                  } else if (getVar('windowMode') === 'EDIT') {
                      setVar('HH_MP_PRESCR_ID', getVar('HH_MP_PRESCR_ID', 1));
                      setVar('FULL_STR', getVar('HH_MP_PRESCR_ID'));
                      executeAction('selectAction', function() {
                          if (!empty(getVar('messageError'))) {
                              // Обработка ситуации, когда редактируем запись  при измененном справочнике
                              D3Api.showAlert(getVar('messageError'));
                          }
                          base().checkActiveDuration();
      
                          if (!empty(getValue('TIME_END'))) {
                              setCaption('TIME_END_HAND', getValue('TIME_END'));
                          }
      
                          setVar('mpDescribeOld', getValue('MP_DESCRIBES'));
                          base().funcMpPrescribesSpeed();
      
                          executeAction('getMTS_DESC', function() {
                              if (getVar('mnnId')) {
                                  Form.setAntitumorState();
                              } else {
                                  base().isCheck(1);
                              }
                              base().measureOnShow();
                          });
      
                          // Инициализация переменных для МНН при загрузке данных EDIT
                          var isMnn = +getVar('MP_CLASS') === 4 || !empty(getVar('mnnId'));
                          setVar('IS_MNN', isMnn);
      
                          if (isMnn) {
                              // Для МНН препаратов
                              setValue('QUANTITY', 1);
                              setValue('ALT_MEASURE_DOSE', null);
      
                              // Скрываем поля для МНН
                              ['ACM_DOSE', 'ACM_DOSE_L', 'ALT_MEASURE_DOSE', 'ALT_MEASURE_CODE',
                               'QUANTITY', 'QUANTITY_L'].forEach(function(name) {
                                  setDomVisible(getControlByName(name), false);
                              });
      
                              // Убираем маски
                              MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', 'QUANTITY');
                              MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', 'ALT_MEASURE_DOSE');
      
                              // Показываем dosageForm и cmbDoseMeasure для МНН
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('dosageForm'), true);
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('cmbDoseMeasure'), true);
      
                          } else {
                              // Для обычных препаратов
                              ['ACM_DOSE', 'ACM_DOSE_L', 'ALT_MEASURE_CODE', 'QUANTITY_L'].forEach(function(name) {
                                  setDomVisible(getControlByName(name), true);
                                  if (name.indexOf('_L') > -1) {
                                      getControlByName(name).style.display = 'inline-block';
                                  }
                              });
      
                              // QUANTITY всегда показываем для обычных с правильным display
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('QUANTITY'), true);
                              getControlByName('QUANTITY').style.display = 'inline-table';
      
                              // ALT_MEASURE_DOSE показываем только если есть альтернативная единица
                              var hasAltMeasure = !empty(getValue('ALT_MEASURE_DOSE')) && !empty(getVar('KOEFF'));
                              if (hasAltMeasure) {
                                  setDomVisible(getControlByName('ALT_MEASURE_DOSE'), true);
                                  getControlByName('ALT_MEASURE_DOSE').style.display = 'inline-table';
                              }
      
                              // Добавляем маски
                              MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', 'QUANTITY');
                              if (hasAltMeasure) {
                                  MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', 'ALT_MEASURE_DOSE');
                              }
      
                              if (empty(getValue('ALT_MEASURE_DOSE'))) {
                                  setValue('ALT_MEASURE_CODE');
                                  setCaption('ALT_MEASURE_CODE');
                              }
      
                              // Скрываем dosageForm и cmbDoseMeasure для обычных препаратов
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('dosageForm'), false);
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('cmbDoseMeasure'), false);
                          }
      
                          if (empty(getValue('ALT_MEASURE_DOSE')) || empty(getVar('KOEFF'))) {
                              base().setEditReadonly('ALT_MEASURE_DOSE', true);
                          } else {
                              base().setEditReadonly('ALT_MEASURE_DOSE', false);
                          }
      
                          setVar('ACM_DOSE_MEASURE', getCaption("ACM_DOSE_L"));
                          refreshDataSet('DS_DATETYPES');
                          refreshDataSet('DS_MP_TYPES');
                          refreshDataSet('DS_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS');
                          base().onchangeMpDescribes();
                          Form.addDescribeListener();
      
                          if (+getVar('MP_CLASS') !== 4) {
                              setVar('MULTI_USE', getValue('NOMMODIF'));
                              executeAction('CHECK_MULTI_USE', function() {
                                  startMultiDataSetsGroup();
                                      // загрузка списка "Способ введения"
                                      refreshDataSet('DS_MED_USE_METHODS');
                                  endMultiDataSetsGroup(0, function() {
                                      if (!empty(getVar('MED_USE_METHOD'))) {
                                          setValue('MED_USE_METHOD', getVar('MED_USE_METHOD'));
                                          setCaption('MED_USE_METHOD', getVar('MED_USE_METHOD_CAP'));
                                      }
                                  });
                              });
                              base().checkComplex();
                          } else {
                              startMultiDataSetsGroup();
                                  // загрузка списка "Способ введения"
                                  refreshDataSet('DS_MED_USE_METHODS');
                              endMultiDataSetsGroup(0, function() {
                                  if (!empty(getVar('MED_USE_METHOD'))) {
                                      setValue('MED_USE_METHOD', getVar('MED_USE_METHOD'));
                                      setCaption('MED_USE_METHOD', getVar('MED_USE_METHOD_CAP'));
                                  }
                              });
                              base().refreshDsTimes();
                          }
      
                          // рассчитываем дозу в зависимости от кол-ва
                          var res = base().delZer(
                              parseToJSFloat(getValue('QUANTITY')) * parseToJSFloat(getVar('REAL_DOSE')) * parseToJSFloat(getVar('DOSE_PACK'))
                          );
      
                          setValue('FIN_DATE_TYPE', getVar('FIN_DATE_TYPE'));
                          base().setDisableFromDescribes();
      
                          if (+getVar('MP_CLASS') === 4) {
                              base().hideNotMnn();
                          } else {
                              setValue('DOSE', res);
                          }
      
                          if (+getVar('MP_CLASS') === 4) {
                              getControlByName('IS_PAT_MED').style.display = 'none';
                          } else {
                              getControlByName('IS_PAT_MED').style.display = '';
                          }
      
                          if (+getVar('isManual') === 1) {
                              setValue('DATE_BEGIN', '');
                              setValue('TIME_BEGIN', '');
                              setValue('DATE_BEGIN_HAND', '');
                              setValue('TIME_BEGIN_HAND', '');
                          }
      
                          startMultiDataSetsGroup();
                              refreshDataSet('dsComboMnn');
                          endMultiDataSetsGroup(0, function() {
                              let data = getDataSet('dsComboMnn').data;
                              let is_combo = data.length > 1;
                              let is_view_dose = (+getVar('D_TYPE') !== 6);
                              setVar('IS_COMBO', +is_combo);
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('trComboMnn'), is_combo);
                              if (!isMnn) {
                                  setDomVisible(getControlByName('ACM_DOSE'), !is_combo);
                              }
      
                              Form.onShowStandartDoseItem(is_view_dose);
      
                              if (!empty(getVar('mnnId'))) {
                                  setValue('QUANTITY', 1);
                              }
      
                              setVar('DOSE', getValue('DOSE'));
                              setVar('QUANTITY', getValue('QUANTITY'));
                              Form.onChangeQuantity();
                          });
                      });
      
                      getControlByName('COMMENTARY').style.display = '';
                      getControlByName('COMM_LABEL').style.display = '';
                      setCaption('OkAppl', 'Подтвердить');
                      setDomVisible(getControlByName('OkButton'), false);
                      setWindowCaption('Лекарственные назначения: редактирование');
                  }
      
                  if (!(getVar('windowMode') === 'EDIT' || getVar('windowMode') === 'COPY')) {
                      Form.addDescribeListener();
                  }
      
                  getPage(0).addListener('onchangepropertyDATE_BEGIN_HAND', function() {
                      if (+getVar('D_TYPE') === 4) {
                          setValue('DATE_BEGIN', getValue('DATE_BEGIN_HAND'));
                          setValue('DATE_CREATE', getValue('DATE_BEGIN_HAND'));
                      }
                  }, false, false);
      
                  getDataSet('DS_DESCR_SCHEDULE').addEventListener('afterrefresh', 'base().afterRefreshDsDescrSchedule()', this);
                  base().addFinDateTypeMasks(+getValue('FIN_DATE_TYPE'));
                  setVar('windowModeReal', getVar('windowMode'));
                  base().onChangeDateOrTimeHand();
              };
      
              Form.changeMaskTimeBeginHand = function() {
                  if (+getVar('D_TYPE') === 4) {
                      MaskInspector_addControl('additMaskIns', 'TIME_BEGIN_HAND');
                  }
              }
              Form.onChangeCheck = function() {
                  if (CheckBox_GetChecked(getControlByName('DURING'))) {
                      Edit_SetEnabled(getControlByName('DURATION'), true);
                      ComboBox_SetEnabled(getControlByName('MEASURE'), true);
                      setAttribute(getControlByName('DURATION'),'emptyMask','true');
                      MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', 'DURATION');
                  } else {
                      base().clearDuration();
                      Edit_SetEnabled(getControlByName('DURATION'), false);
                      ComboBox_SetEnabled(getControlByName('MEASURE'), false);
                      setAttribute(getControlByName('DURATION'),'emptyMask','false');
                      MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', 'DURATION');
                  }
              };
      
              Form.isCheck = function(auto) {
                  if (getVar('oldAntitumorDrug') !== getValue('ANTITUMOR_DRUG')) {
                      if (+getValue('ANTITUMOR_DRUG') === 1) {
                          setValue('canEditComplex', '1');
                          Form.checkEditComplex();
                      }
                      setVar('oldAntitumorDrug', getValue('ANTITUMOR_DRUG'));
                  }
                  if (+getValue('ANTITUMOR_DRUG') === 1) {
                      setDomVisible(getControlByName('TR_MTS'), true);
                      setDomVisible(getControlByName('btnCalcDoseDrug'), true);
      
                      if (+getVar('EXEC_MTS') === 1) {
                          executeAction('requireMTS', function() {
                              if (getVar('REQUIRE_MTS') == 1) {
                                  MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', 'MTS_DESC');
                              }
                          });
                      } else {
                          if (+getVar('REQUIRE_MTS') === 1) {
                              MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', 'MTS_DESC');
                          }
                      }
                      if (!empty(getValue('NOMMODIF')) && auto === 1) {
                          setEnabled('ANTITUMOR_DRUG', !+getVar('IsUnEditableOnko'));
                      }
                  } else {
                      MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', 'MTS_DESC');
                      setDomVisible(getControlByName('TR_MTS'), false);
                      setDomVisible(getControlByName('btnCalcDoseDrug'), false);
                      clearControl('MTS_DESC');
                      setVar('MTS_DESC_CODE', '');
                      if (!empty(getValue('NOMMODIF')) && auto === 1) {
                          setEnabled('ANTITUMOR_DRUG', true);
                      }
                  }
              };
      
              Form.refreshExtComplex = function(nameDataSet, nameGroup) {
                  Form.oldNommodif[nameGroup] = [];
      
                  getRepeaterByGroupName(nameGroup).clone.clones.forEach(function(c) {
                      $$(c.clone);
                          Form.oldNommodif[nameGroup].push({
                              'id': c.data['NOMMODIF_ID'],
                              'name': c.data['NOMMODIF_NAME'],
                              'Dose_c': getValue('Dose_c'),
                              'QantDose_c': getValue('QantDose_c'),
                              'AltDose_c': getValue('AltDose_c'),
                          });
                      _$$();
                  });
                  refreshDataSet(nameDataSet);
              };
      
              Form.checkComplex = function() {
                  if (!empty(getValue('NOMMODIF'))) {
                      executeAction('IS_COMPLEX', function() {
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('divCanEditComplex'), (+getVar('IS_COMPLEX') === 1));
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('signReduction'), +getVar('IS_COMPLEX') !== 1);
                          if (empty(getVar('noExtempComplex')) && +getVar('IS_COMPLEX') !== 1 && +getVar('D_TYPE') !== 6) {
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('ExtempoInit'), true);
                          } else {
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('ExtempoInit'), false);
                          }
      
                          if (+getVar('IS_COMPLEX') === 1) {
                              Form.refreshExtComplex('DS_COMPLEX', 'complexgroup');
                              getControlByName('ComplexBlock').style.display = empty(getVar('noExtempComplex')) ? '' : 'none';
                              getControlByName('ExtempoBlock').style.display = 'none';
                              base().recountDose(1, 'DOSE_QUANT', 'AMOUNT', getValue('DOSE'));
                              if (+getVar('D_TYPE') === 6) {
                                  setValue('MP_DESCRIBES', null);
                                  setCaption('MP_DESCRIBES', null);
                              }
                          } else {
                              getControlByName('ComplexBlock').style.display = 'none';
      
                              if (!empty(getVar('HH_MP_PRESCR_ID'))) {
                                  startMultiDataSetsGroup();
                                      Form.refreshExtComplex('DS_EXTEMPO', 'extempogroup');
                                  endMultiDataSetsGroup(0, function() {
                                      var data = getDataSet('DS_EXTEMPO').data,
                                          is_extempo = data.length >= 1;
      
                                      if (+getVar('D_TYPE') !== 6 && is_extempo) {
                                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('ExtempoBlock'), true);
                                      }
                                  });
                              }
      
                              if (+getVar('D_TYPE') === 6) {
                                  getControlByName('ExtempoBlock').style.display = 'none';
      
                                  if (!empty(getVar('HH_MP_PRESCR_ID')) && +getVar('D_TYPE_OLD') === 6 &&
                                      +getVar('mpDescribeOld') === +getValue('MP_DESCRIBES')) {
                                      refreshDataSet('DS_SCHEDULE');
                                  }
                              }
                          }
                          base().checkActiveDuration();
                          base().refreshDsTimes();
                      });
                  } else {
                      setVar('IS_COMPLEX', 0);
                      getControlByName('ComplexBlock').style.display = 'none';
      
                      if (!empty(getVar('HH_MP_PRESCR_ID'))) {
                          startMultiDataSetsGroup();
                              Form.refreshExtComplex('DS_EXTEMPO', 'extempogroup');
                          endMultiDataSetsGroup(0, function() {
                              var data = getDataSet('DS_EXTEMPO').data,
                                  is_extempo = data.length >= 1;
      
                              if (+getVar('D_TYPE') !== 6 && is_extempo) {
                                  setDomVisible(getControlByName('ExtempoBlock'), true);
                              }
                          });
                      }
      
                      if (+getVar('D_TYPE') === 6) {
                          getControlByName('ExtempoBlock').style.display = 'none';
      
                          if (!empty(getVar('HH_MP_PRESCR_ID')) && +getVar('D_TYPE_OLD') === 6 &&
                              +getVar('mpDescribeOld') === +getValue('MP_DESCRIBES')) {
                              refreshDataSet('DS_SCHEDULE');
                          }
                      }
                  }
              };
      
              Form.checkEditComplex = function() {
                  if (+getVar('IS_COMPLEX') === 1) {
                      if (+getValue('canEditComplex') === 1) {
                          getControlByName('StandartDoseItem').style.display = 'none';
                          let clones = getRepeaterByGroupName('complexgroup').clone.clones;
                          for (let i = 0; i < clones.length; i++) {
                              $$(clones[i].clone);
                                  setEnabled('Dose_c', true);
                                  setEnabled('AltDose_c', !empty(clones[i].clone.clone.data['ALT_DOSE']) && !empty(clones[i].clone.clone.data['KOEFF']));
                                  setEnabled('QantDose_c', true);
                                  setDomVisible(getControlByName('editDose_c'), true);
                              _$$();
                          }
                      } else {
                          getControlByName('StandartDoseItem').style.display = 'table-row';
                          let clones = getRepeaterByGroupName('complexgroup').clone.clones;
                          for (let i = 0; i < clones.length; i++) {
                              $$(clones[i].clone);
                                  setEnabled('Dose_c', false);
                                  setEnabled('AltDose_c', false);
                                  setEnabled('QantDose_c', false);
                                  setDomVisible(getControlByName('editDose_c'), false);
                              _$$();
                          }
                      }
                  }
              };
      
              Form.refreshDsTimes = function() {
                  // Для рефреша обязательно должна быть сабка ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/TimeHandSubform Ý
                  if (+getVar('D_TYPE') === 4) {
                      if (!empty(getVar('HH_MP_PRESCR_ID')) && +getVar('D_TYPE_OLD') === 4) {
                          refreshDataSet('DS_TIMES');
                      }
                      base().onChangeDateOrTimeHand();
                      Form.maskEmp(false);
                  }
              };
      
              Form.clearDuration = function() {
                  if (!CheckBox_GetChecked(getControlByName('DURING'))) {
                      Edit_SetValue(getControlByName('DURATION'),'');
                      ComboBox_SetValue(getControlByName('MEASURE'),'');
                      setVar('MEASURE','');
                  }
              }
              Form.processStore = function() {
                  if (!CheckBox_GetChecked(getControlByName('DURING'))) {
                      ComboBox_SetValue(getControlByName('MEASURE'),'');
                  } else {
                      setVar('MEASURE', ComboBox_GetValue(getControlByName('MEASURE')));
                  };
                  var prefix = getVar('ACTIVE_TIMEBLOCK') === 'main' ? '' : 'TH_';
                  setVar('FIN_DATE_TYPE', getValue(prefix + 'FIN_DATE_TYPE'));
                  setVar('MESSAGE', null);
                  if (getVar('FIN_DATE_TYPE') == 0 && (getVar('D_TYPE') != 4) && (empty(getValue('DATE_END')) || empty(getValue('TIME_END')))) {
                      alert('Не заданы дата или время завершения назначения!');
                      return;
                  }
                  // если время вручную было задано, добавляем его в репитер перед сохранением
                  var clonesTimes = getRepeaterByGroupName('MpTimes').clone.clones;
                  var clonesCount = clonesTimes.length;
                  if (empty(getValue('TIME_BEGIN_HAND')) && !clonesCount && getVar('D_TYPE') == 4) {
                      alert('Не задано время исполнения!');
                      return;
                  }
                  var clonesShCount = getRepeaterByGroupName('MpSchedule').clone.clones.length;
                  if (getVar('D_TYPE') == 6) {
                      if (!clonesShCount) {
                          alert('Не задан график исполнения!');
                          return;
                      } else {
                          if (+getVar('FIN_DATE_TYPE') === 1 && +getVar('SCHEDULE_DAYS')) {
                              setValue('TIME_END', getValue('TIME_BEGIN'));
                          }
                      }
                  }
                  if (+getVar('FIN_DATE_TYPE') === 1 && empty(getVar('DAYSCOUNT'))) {
                      alert('Не задано количество дней назначения!');
                      return;
                  }
                  // Для добавления в репитер обязательно должна быть сабка ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/TimeHandSubform Ý
                  if (+getVar('D_TYPE') === 4 && !empty(getValue('TIME_BEGIN_HAND'))) {
                      base().addTime();
                      base().onChangeDateOrTimeHand();
                  }
      
                  // Ищем минимальное время в репитерах
                  if (clonesTimes.length > 0) {
                      setVar('minTime', base().findMinTime(clonesTimes));
                  }
                  // TODO доделать, когда добавятся новые MP_CLASS
                  if (+getVar('MP_CLASS') !== 4) {
                      if (+getVar('IS_COMPLEX') === 1) {
                          setVar('MP_CLASS', 1);
                      } else if (getCloneObjectsByRepeaterName('EXTEMPO', 'ExtempoDel').length > 0) {
                          setVar('MP_CLASS', 2);
                      } else if (+getVar('IS_COMBO') === 1) {
                          setVar('MP_CLASS', 5);
                      } else {
                          setVar('MP_CLASS', 0);
                      }
                  }
                  base().recountScheduleDays();
                  if (!empty(getValue('NOMMODIF'))) {
                      executeAction('getMessage', function() {
                          base().processStoreSecondStep();
                      });
                  } else {
                      base().processStoreSecondStep();
                  }
              }
              Form.processStoreSecondStep = function() {
                  if (!empty(getVar('MESSAGE'))) {
                      showConfirm(getVar('MESSAGE'), 'Предупреждение', 650, 150, function() {
                          setVar('MESSAGE', null);
                          base().processStoreSecondStep();
                      }, null)
                  }
                  if (!empty(getVar('ERR'))) {
                      if (getVar('UseAllergenNommodif') == 2) {
                          showAlert('Невозможно назначение или списание препарата. ' + getVar('ERR') + '.', 'Ошибка');
                          return;
                      }
                      else if (getVar('UseAllergenNommodif') == 1) {
                          showConfirm(getVar('ERR') + '. Продолжить назначение?', 'Предупреждение', 650, 150,
                          function() {
