                          D3Api.showAlert("Нельзя выбрать периодичность с данным типом для экстемпорального назначения");
                          setValue('MP_DESCRIBES', null);
                          setCaption('MP_DESCRIBES', '');
                          return;
                      }
      
                      getControlByName('HandTimeBlock').style.display = 'none';
                      getControlByName('MainTimeBlock').style.display = '';
                      getControlByName('ScheduleItemsBlock').style.display = '';
                      getControlByName('ScheduleAddItem').style.display = '';
                      getControlByName('StandartDoseItem').style.display = 'none';
                      getControlByName('ComplexBlock').style.display = 'none';
                      getControlByName('ExtempoBlock').style.display = 'none';
                      getRepeaterByGroupName('extempogroup').killClones();
                      if (getVar('actionBtn') !== 'CORRECT') {
                          _setFocus(getControlByName('DATE_BEGIN'));
                      }
                      if (!empty(getVar('HH_MP_PRESCR_ID')) && (+getVar('D_TYPE_OLD') === 6) &&
                          +getVar('mpDescribeOld') === +getValue('MP_DESCRIBES')) {
                          refreshDataSet('DS_SCHEDULE');
                      } else {
                          refreshDataSet('DS_DESCR_SCHEDULE');
                      }
                  } else {
                      getControlByName('HandTimeBlock').style.display = 'none';
                      getControlByName('MainTimeBlock').style.display = '';
                      getControlByName('ScheduleItemsBlock').style.display = 'none';
                      getControlByName('ScheduleAddItem').style.display = 'none';
                      if (+getVar('IS_COMBO') === 1) {
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('trComboMnn'), true);
                      } else {
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('trComboMnn'), false);
                          MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', 'DOSE');
                      }
                      setVar('ACTIVE_TIMEBLOCK', 'main');
                  }
                  if (!empty(getVar('mnnId'))) {
                      if (+getVar('IS_COMBO') === 1) {
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('trComboMnn'), true);
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('StandartDoseItem'), true);
                      } else {
                          if (+getVar('D_TYPE') === 6) {
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('StandartDoseItem'), false);
                              MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', 'cmbDoseMeasure');
                              MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', 'DOSE');
                          } else {
                              getControlByName('StandartDoseItem').style.display = 'table-row';
                              MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', 'cmbDoseMeasure');
                              MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', 'DOSE');
                          }
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('trComboMnn'), false);
                      }
                  }
                  base().onChangeDateOrTimeHand();
                  Form.onShowStandartDoseItem();
              };
      
              Form.selectNommodiffExtempo = function(_dom, _clone) {
                  var win;
                  if (empty(getVar('windowMode'))) {
                      win = openWindow({
                          name: 'ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/goodsupply_select',
                          vars: {
                              'BeginAppoint' : getValue('DATE_BEGIN'),
                              'processStore': 1
                          }
                      }, true, 800, 600);
                  } else {
                      win = openWindow({
                          name: 'ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/nommodif_select',
                          vars: {
                              'HH_DEP_ID': getVar('HH_DEP'),
                              'HH_DEP_LYING': getVar('HH_DEP_LYING'),
                              'NO_COMPLEX': 1,
                              'PAYMENT_KIND_ID': getVar('PAYMENT_KIND_ID'),
                              'processStore': 1,
                              'hideMnn': 1
                          }
                      }, true, 800, 730);
                  }
                  win.addListener('onafterclose', function(mod) {
                      if (+mod['ModalResult'] === 1) {
                          setVar('DOSE_PACK', mod['DOSE_PACK']);
                          setVar('vHideMnn', +!empty(mod['NOMMODIF_NAME']));
                          Form.closeNommoDiff(mod);
                          Form.onChangeQuantityInit(mod);
                          if (empty(mod['mnnId'])) {
                              $$(_clone);
                                  setValue('RealDose_c', base().delZer(parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE'])));
                                  setValue('Dose_c', getValue('RealDose_c'));
                                  setValue('QantDose_c', base().delZer(((parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE']) / parseToJSFloat(mod['REAL_DOSE'])) / parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE_PACK']))));
                                  setCaption('NOM_DOSE', mod['REAL_DOSE']);
                                  setCaption('Dose_m', mod['DOSE_MEASURE_NAME']);
                                  setCaption('QantDose_m', mod['MAIN_MEASURE_CODE']);
                                  setValue('ColDose', base().delZer(parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE']) / parseToJSFloat(mod['REAL_DOSE'])));
                                  setValue('extempoNOMMODIF', mod['return_id']);
                                  setCaption('extempoNOMMODIF', mod['NOMMODIF_NAME']);
                                  if (!empty(mod['ALT_MEASURE_CODE']) && !empty(mod['KOEFF'])) {
                                      base().setEditReadonly('AltDose_c', false);
                                      setCaption('AltDose_m', mod['ALT_MEASURE_CODE']);
                                      setValue('AltDose_c', base().delZer(parseToJSFloat(getValue('QantDose_c')) * parseToJSFloat(mod['KOEFF'])));
                                  } else {
                                      setCaption('AltDose_m', '');
                                      setValue('AltDose_c', null);
                                      base().setEditReadonly('AltDose_c', true);
                                  }
                                  setCaption('KOEFF_C', mod['KOEFF']);
                                  setCaption('DOSE_PACK_C', mod['DOSE_PACK']);
                              _$$();
                          } else {
                              // Если выбран МНН препарат
                              $$(_clone);
                                  setValue('RealDose_c', base().delZer(parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE'])));
                                  setValue('Dose_c', getValue('RealDose_c'));
                                  setValue('QantDose_c', 1); // Для МНН всегда 1
                                  setCaption('NOM_DOSE', mod['REAL_DOSE']);
                                  setCaption('Dose_m', mod['DOSE_MEASURE_NAME']);
                                  setCaption('QantDose_m', mod['MAIN_MEASURE_CODE']);
                                  setValue('ColDose', base().delZer(parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE']) / parseToJSFloat(mod['REAL_DOSE'])));
                                  setValue('extempoNOMMODIF', mod['return_id']);
                                  setCaption('extempoNOMMODIF', mod['NOMMODIF_NAME']);
                                  // Для МНН ALT_DOSE = null
                                  setCaption('AltDose_m', '');
                                  setValue('AltDose_c', null);
                                  base().setEditReadonly('AltDose_c', true);
                                  setCaption('KOEFF_C', mod['KOEFF']);
                                  setCaption('DOSE_PACK_C', mod['DOSE_PACK']);
                              _$$();
                          }
                      }
                  });
              };
      
              Form.ExtempoAddClone = function() {
                  var win;
                  if (empty(getVar('windowMode'))) {
                      win = openWindow({
                          name: 'ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/goodsupply_select',
                          vars: {
                              'BeginAppoint' : getValue('DATE_BEGIN'),
                              'processStore': 1
                          }
                      }, true, 800, 600);
                  } else {
                      win = openWindow({
                          name: 'ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/nommodif_select',
                          vars: {
                              'HH_DEP_ID': getVar('HH_DEP'),
                              'HH_DEP_LYING': getVar('HH_DEP_LYING'),
                              'NO_COMPLEX': 1,
                              'PAYMENT_KIND_ID': getVar('PAYMENT_KIND_ID'),
                              'processStore': 1,
                              'hideMnn': 1,
                              'viewToExpand': 1,
                              'schemeDescId': getValue('MTS_DESC')
                          }
                      }, true, 800, 730);
                  }
                  win.addListener('onafterclose', function(mod) {
                      if (+mod['ModalResult'] === 1) {
                          Form.closeNommoDiff(mod);
                          var clones = getRepeaterByGroupName('extempogroup').clone.clones;
                          var err = 0;
      
                          // проверяем уникальность препаратов в составе экстемпорального назначения
                          Array.prototype.forEach.call(clones, function(clone) {
                              if (+clone.data['NOMMODIF_ID'] === +mod['return_id']) {
                                  err = 1;
                              }
                          });
      
                          if (+getValue('NOMMODIF') === +mod['return_id']) {
                              err = 1;
                          }
      
                          if (err === 1) {
                              showAlert('Выбранный препарат уже присутствует в назначении.', 'Ошибка', 310, 100);
                              return;
                          } else {
                              var data = {};
                              data['DOSE'] = base().delZer(parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE']));
                              data['NOM_DOSE'] = mod['REAL_DOSE'];
                              data['QUANTITY_DOSE'] = base().delZer(((parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE']) / parseToJSFloat(mod['REAL_DOSE'])) / parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE_PACK'])));
                              data['COL_DOSE'] = base().delZer(parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE']) / parseToJSFloat(mod['REAL_DOSE']));
                              data['CHECK_REPLACE'] = mod['CHECK_REPLACE'];
                              data['DOSE_MES'] = mod['DOSE_MEASURE_NAME'];
                              data['QUANTITY_DOSE_MES'] = mod['MAIN_MEASURE_CODE'];
                              data['NOMMODIF_ID'] = mod['return_id'];
                              data['NOMMODIF_NAME'] = mod['NOMMODIF_NAME'];
                              setVar('vHideMnn', +!empty(mod['NOMMODIF_NAME']));
                              if (!empty(mod['ALT_MEASURE_CODE']) && !empty(mod['KOEFF'])) {
                                  data['ALT_DOSE_MES'] = mod['ALT_MEASURE_CODE'];
                                  data['ALT_DOSE'] = base().delZer((1 / parseToJSFloat(mod['DOSE_PACK'])) * parseToJSFloat(mod['KOEFF']));
                              } else {
                                  data['ALT_DOSE_MES'] = '';
                                  data['ALT_DOSE'] = null;
                              }
                              data['KOEFF'] = mod['KOEFF'];
                              data['DOSE_PACK'] = mod['DOSE_PACK'];
      
                              getControlByName('ExtempoBlock').style.display = '';
                              addRepeaterClone('extempogroup', data, getControlByName('ExtempoAddBlock'));
                              base().ExtempoShowHide(true);
                          }
                      }
                  });
              };
      
              Form.ExtempoDelClone = function(ctrl) {
                  removeRepeaterClone('extempogroup', ctrl);
                  if (getCloneObjectsByRepeaterName('EXTEMPO', 'ExtempoDel').length == 0) {
                      base().ExtempoShowHide(false);
                  }
              };
      
              Form.ExtempoShowHide = function(show) {
                  setDomVisible(getControlByName('ExtempoInit'), !show);
                  setDomVisible(getControlByName('ExtempoAddBlock'), show);
                  setVar('vHideMnn', +show);
              };
      
              Form.ExtempoInit = function() {
                  base().ExtempoAddClone();
              };
      
              Form.RemoveScheduleItem = function(item) {
                  function delMask(e) {
                      MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', e);
                  };
                  $$(item);
                      ['SCH_DOSE', 'SCH_DOSE_QU', 'SCH_TIME'].forEach(delMask);
                  _$$();
                  removeRepeaterClone('MpSchedule',item);
              };
      
              Form.AddScheduleItem = function(stime, dom, delMPPresc = 0) {
      			setVar('delMPPresc',delMPPresc);
                  $$(dom);
                      var clone = addRepeaterClone('MpSchedule', {
                          SCHEDULE_DOSE: getValue('DOSE'),
                          SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT: getValue("ALT_MEASURE_DOSE"),
                          SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU: getValue("QUANTITY"),
                          SCHEDULE_DOSE_L: getCaption("DOSE_L"),
                          SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT_L: getCaption("ALT_MEASURE_CODE"),
                          SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU_L: getCaption("QUANTITY_L"),
                          SCH_TIME: stime
                      }, dom, null);
                  _$$();
                  getControlByName('IS_PAT_MED').style.display = '';
                  getControlByName('COMMENTARY').style.display = '';
                  getControlByName('COMM_LABEL').style.display = '';
                  setCaption('OkButton', 'Назначить и продолжить');
              };
      
              Form.DuplicateScheduleItem = function(item) {
                  var pos = getControlByName('SCHEDULE_ADD');
                  $$(item);
                  var clone = addRepeaterClone('MpSchedule', {
                      SCHEDULE_DOSE: getValue("SCH_DOSE"),
                      SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT: getValue("SCH_DOSE_ALT"),
                      SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU: getValue("SCH_DOSE_QU"),
                      SCHEDULE_DOSE_L: getCaption("DOSE_L"),
                      SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT_L: getCaption("ALT_MEASURE_CODE"),
                      SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU_L: getCaption("QUANTITY_L"),
                      SCH_TIME: '00:00'
                  }, pos);
                  _$$();
              };
      
              Form.afterrefreshDsSchedule = function() {
                  refreshDataSet('DS_DESCR_SCHEDULE');
              }
      
              Form.afterRefreshDsDescrSchedule = function() {
                  var clone = getRepeaterByGroupName('MpSchedule');
                  var clones = clone.data.slice(0);
                  clone.killClones();
                  var data = getDataSet('DS_DESCR_SCHEDULE').data;
      
                  if (data.length == 0) {
                      getControlByName('SCHEDULE_ADD').style.display = '';
                      base().AddScheduleItem('00:00', this);
                  } else {
                      getControlByName('SCHEDULE_ADD').style.display = 'none';
      
                      for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
                          base().AddScheduleItem(data[i].D_TIME_STR, this);
                      }
                  }
              };
      
              Form.onPostCloneSchedule = function(_clone, _data, _ctrls) {
                  function addMask(e) {
                      //На время выяснения всей информации для тестирования
                      MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', e);
                  };
      
                  $$(_clone);
                      ['SCH_DOSE', 'SCH_DOSE_QU', 'SCH_TIME'].forEach(addMask);
                      if (+getVar('D_TYPE') === 6 && +getVar('CNT_MP_DESC_TIMES') === 1) {
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('SCHEDULE_DEL'), true);
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('SCHEDULE_ADD'), true);
                          base().setEditReadonly('SCH_TIME', false);
                      } else {
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('SCHEDULE_COPY'), false);
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('SCHEDULE_DEL'), false);
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('SCHEDULE_ADD'), false);
                          base().setEditReadonly('SCH_TIME', true);
                      }
                      if (+getVar('MP_CLASS') === 4 || !empty(getVar('mnnId'))) {
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('SCHEDULE_DOSE_L'), false);
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('SCH_DOSE_ALT'), false);
                          setDomVisible(getControlByName('SCH_DOSE_QU'), false);
                      }
                  _$$();
              };
      
              Form.recountScheduleFields = function(param, cmp) {
                  if (empty(getValue(cmp)) || empty(getVar('REAL_DOSE') || getVar('REAL_DOSE') === "0")) {
                      return;
                  }
      
                  switch (param) {
                      case 1: /*SCH_DOSE*/
                          var res = base().delZer((parseToJSFloat(getValue('SCH_DOSE')) / parseToJSFloat(getVar('REAL_DOSE'))) / parseToJSFloat(getVar('DOSE_PACK')));
                          setValue('SCH_DOSE_QU', res);
      
                          if (!empty(getValue('SCH_DOSE_ALT')) && !empty(getVar('KOEFF'))) {
                              var res = base().delZer(parseToJSFloat(getValue('SCH_DOSE_QU')) * parseToJSFloat(getVar('KOEFF')));
                              setValue('SCH_DOSE_ALT', res);
                          } else {
                              setValue('SCH_DOSE_ALT', null);
                          }
                          break;
                      case 2:/*SCH_DOSE_ALT*/
                          if (empty(getValue('SCH_DOSE_ALT')) || empty(getVar('KOEFF'))) break;
                          var res = base().delZer(
                                  parseToJSFloat(getValue('SCH_DOSE_ALT')) / parseToJSFloat(getVar('KOEFF'))
                          );
                          setValue('SCH_DOSE_QU', res);
                          var res = base().delZer(
                                  parseToJSFloat(getValue('SCH_DOSE_QU')) * parseToJSFloat(getVar('REAL_DOSE')) * parseToJSFloat(getVar('DOSE_PACK'))
                          );
                          setValue('SCH_DOSE', res);
                          break;
                      case 3:/*SCH_DOSE_QU*/
                          var res = base().delZer(
                                  parseToJSFloat(getValue('SCH_DOSE_QU')) * parseToJSFloat(getVar('REAL_DOSE')) * parseToJSFloat(getVar('DOSE_PACK'))
                          );
                          setValue('SCH_DOSE', res);
                          if (!empty(getValue('SCH_DOSE_ALT')) && !empty(getVar('KOEFF'))) {
                              var res = base().delZer(
                                  parseToJSFloat(getValue('SCH_DOSE_QU')) * parseToJSFloat(getVar('KOEFF'))
                              );
                              setValue('SCH_DOSE_ALT', res);
                          } else setValue('SCH_DOSE_ALT', null);
                          break;
                  }
              };
      
              Form.recountScheduleDays = function() {
                  var date_type = getValue('FIN_DATE_TYPE');
                  var db = getValue('DATE_BEGIN');
                  var de = getValue('DATE_END');
                  var time = null;
                  var days = 0;
      
                  if(date_type == 0) {
                      if (!db || !de) {
                          days = -1;
                      } else {
                          db = new Date(db.replace(/(\d{2})\.(\d{2})\.(\d{4})/,'$3-$2-$1'));
                          de = new Date(de.replace(/(\d{2})\.(\d{2})\.(\d{4})/,'$3-$2-$1'));
                          if (db > de) {
                              days = -1;
                          } else {
                              time = de.getTime() - db.getTime();
                              days = Math.floor(time / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
                          }
                      }
                      setVar('SCHEDULE_DAYS', days > 0 ? days : -1);
                  } else if(date_type == 1) {
                      days = getValue('DAYSCOUNT');
                      setVar('SCHEDULE_DAYS', days > 0 ? days : -1);
                  } else {
                      executeAction('getHHEndDate', function() {
                          if(empty(getVar('HH_END_DATE'))) {
                              days = -1;
                              setVar('SCHEDULE_DAYS', days > 0 ? days : -1);
                          } else {
                              db = new Date(db.replace(/(\d{2})\.(\d{2})\.(\d{4})/,'$3-$2-$1'));
                              de = new Date(getVar('HH_END_DATE').replace(/(\d{2})\.(\d{2})\.(\d{4})/,'$3-$2-$1'));
                              time = de.getTime() - db.getTime();
                              days = Math.floor(time / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
                              setVar('SCHEDULE_DAYS', days > 0 ? days : -1);
                          }
                      });
                  }
              };
      
              Form.clearMtsDesc = function() {
                  clearControl('MTS_DESC');
                  setVar('MTS_DESC_CODE', '');
                  MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', 'MTS_DESC');
              };
      
              Form.getCalcDoseDrug = function(_dom) {
                  executeAction('getDataForSchema', function() {
                      let nommodifId = getValue('NOMMODIF');
                      let isPart = false;
                      if (_dom.getAttribute('name') === 'editDose_c') {
                          let cl = getCloneByNameFromControl(_dom, 'COMPLEX');
                          if (cl) {
                              nommodifId = cl.clone.data['NOMMODIF_ID'];
                              isPart = true;
                          }
                      }
                      openD3Form('ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_calc_dose_drug', true, {
                          width: 500,
                          height: 150,
                          vars: {
                              NOMMODIF: nommodifId,
                              AGENT: getVar('AGENT_ID')
                          },
                          onclose: function(mod) {
                              if (mod && +mod.ModalResult === 1) {
                                  if (isPart) {
                                      let ctrlNames = {
                                          'DOSE': ['Dose_c', 1],
                                          'ALT_MEASURE_DOSE': ['AltDose_c', 2],
                                          'QUANTITY': ['QantDose_c', 3],
                                      };
                                      let cl = getCloneByNameFromControl(_dom, 'COMPLEX');
                                      if (mod.returnCode in ctrlNames && cl) {
                                          $$(cl);
                                              Form.CTRLO[ctrlNames[mod.returnCode][0]] = parseToJSFloat(getValue(ctrlNames[mod.returnCode][0]));
                                              setValue(ctrlNames[mod.returnCode][0], mod.returnValue + '');
                                              Form.recountRepeaterFields(ctrlNames[mod.returnCode][1], ctrlNames[mod.returnCode][0]);
                                          _$$();
                                      }
                                  } else {
                                      Form.CTRLO[mod.returnCode] = parseToJSFloat(getValue(mod.returnCode));
                                      setValue(mod.returnCode, mod.returnValue + '');
                                      Form.recountFields(mod.returnCode === 'DOSE' ? 1 : 2, mod.returnCode);
                                  }
                              }
                          }
                      });
                  });
              };
      
              // Сделать некоторые поля нередактируемыми
              Form.setDisableFromDescribes = function() {
                  /*
                  * по времени вручную
                  *  +getVar('D_TYPE') === 4
                  * по графику (с временным интервалом)
                  *  +getVar('D_TYPE') === 6
                  *  +getVar('CNT_MP_DESC_TIMES') === 2
                  * по графику (без временного интервала)
                  *  +getVar('D_TYPE') === 6
                  *  +getVar('CNT_MP_DESC_TIMES') === 1
                  *
                  * DATE_BEGIN_HAND - Назначить на
                  * TIME_BEGIN_HAND - Время
                  * TH_FIN_DATE_TYPE - Назначить по (выпадашка)
                  * DATE_END_HAND - Назначить по (дата)
                  * TIME_END_HAND - Назначить по (время)
                  * MP_DESCRIBES - Периодичность
                  * NOMMODIF - Препарат
                  * DATE_BEGIN - Назначить с (дата)
                  * TIME_BEGIN - Назначить с (время)
                  * FIN_DATE_TYPE - Назначить по (выпадашка)
                  * DATE_END - Назначить по (дата)
                  * TIME_END - Назначить по (время)
                  * */
                  if (getVar('windowModeReal') === 'EDIT' || getVar('windowModeReal') === 'COPY') {
                      // Ý костыль для пересчёта, когда ALT_MEASURE_DOSE с запятой и кнопка "Подтвердить" серая
                      if (!empty(getValue('ALT_MEASURE_DOSE')) && !empty(getValue('QUANTITY'))) {
                          base().recountFields(3,'QUANTITY');
                      }
                      setEnabled('NOMMODIF', false);
                  }
              };
      
              // Вычисляем количество доступных записей и обновляем датасет
              Form.funcMpPrescribesSpeed = function() {
                  setVar('MEASURE', getValue('MEASURE'));

                          // Если связь D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES.DOSE_MEASURE_ID и D_FED_NSI_LINK_SP
                          if (!empty(getVar('fedNsiDoseMeasures'))) {
                              // Показываем выпадашку "Ед. изм. скорости введения"
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('divSpeed'), true);
                              // Добавляем обязательность
                              setAttribute(getControlByName('ctrlSpeed'),'emptyMask','true');
                              // С одной маской не работает, с двумя работает Ý
                              MaskInspector_addControl('additMaskIns', 'ctrlSpeed');
                              MaskInspector_addControl('MainMI', 'ctrlSpeed');
                              refreshDataSet('dsMpPrescribesSpeed');
                          } else {
                              setValue('ctrlSpeed', '');
                              setDomVisible(getControlByName('divSpeed'), false);
                              MaskInspector_delControl('additMaskIns', 'ctrlSpeed');
                              MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', 'ctrlSpeed');
                              setVar('fedNsiDoseMeasures', '');
                          }
                      });
                  } else {
                      setValue('ctrlSpeed', '');
                      setDomVisible(getControlByName('divSpeed'), false);
                      MaskInspector_delControl('additMaskIns', 'ctrlSpeed');
                      MaskInspector_delControl('MainMI', 'ctrlSpeed');
                      setVar('fedNsiDoseMeasures', '');
                  }
              };

              Form.onChangeQuantity = function() {
                  var clones = getRepeaterByGroupName('rptComboMNN').clone.clones;
                  const doseQuantValue = parseToJSFloat(getValue('DOSE_QUANT'));
      
                  for (var i = 0; i < clones.length; i++) {
                      $$(clones[i].clone);
                          // Формула: dose_quant * d_nommodif_acm.dose
                          var doseAcm = doseQuantValue * parseToJSFloat(clones[i].data.DOSE);
      
                          if (+doseAcm === 0) {
                              setValue('eDoseAcm', '');
                          } else {
                              // Округляем до 3 знаков, если есть дробная часть
                              doseAcm = doseAcm % 1 ? parseToJSFloat(doseAcm.toFixed(3)) : doseAcm;
                              doseAcm = parseToOracleFloat(doseAcm);
                              setValue('eDoseAcm', doseAcm);
                          }
                      _$$();
                  }
              };

  [2] M2 Action: checkNSIAndAccess
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              begin
                -- :FED_NSI_DOSE_MEASURES - Связь FN_DOSE_MEASURES и D_DOSE_MEASURES
                :FED_NSI_DOSE_MEASURES := D_PKG_FED_NSI_LINKS.GET_CURRENT_VAL(pnRAISE       => 0,
                                                                              pnLPU         => :LPU,
                                                                              psFN_UNITCODE => 'FN_DOSE_MEASURES',
                                                                              psUNITCODE    => 'DOSE_MEASURES',
                                                                              psUNIT_ID     => :DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                                                                              psFIELD       => 'ID',
                                                                              pnUSE_CACHE   => 1);
      
                begin
                  -- :CNT_MEASURES_SPEED - Подсчёт количества записей с проверкой на префиксы и постфиксы
                  select count(1)
                    into :CNT_MEASURES_SPEED
                    from D_V_MEASURES ms
                   where ms.VERSION =
                         (select D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'MEASURES')
                            from dual)
                     and exists (select null
                                   from D_V_CATALOGS c
                                  where c.ID = ms.CID
                                    and c.C_UNITCODE = 'MEASURES'
                                    and c.C_NAME = 'Скорость введения')
                     and exists (select null
                                   from D_V_DOSE_MEASURES dm
                                  where dm.ID = :DOSE_MEASURE_ID
                                    and regexp_replace(ms.MNEMOCODE, '/[^/]*$', '') = dm.MNEMOCODE)
                     and regexp_substr(ms.MNEMOCODE, '\/([^\/]+)$', 1, 1, NULL, 1) =
                         case when coalesce(:MEASURE_VAR, case when :DURING = '1' then :MEASURE_CTRL
                                                               else null
                                                          end) = 'HOUR' then 'час'
                              else 'мин'
                         end;
                end;
              end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_DOSE_MEASURES;
          D_V_MEASURES;
          D_V_CATALOGS;
      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU;
          D_PKG_FED_NSI_LINKS.GET_CURRENT_VAL;

  [3] M2 DataSet: dsMpPrescribesSpeed
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              select ms.ID,
                     ms.M_NAME
                from D_V_MEASURES ms
               where ms.VERSION = (select D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(0, :LPU, 'MEASURES')
                                     from dual)
                 -- Если нет одного совпадения и есть каталог, выводим всё из каталога
                 and ((:CNT_MEASURES_SPEED > 1 or :CNT_MEASURES_SPEED = 0)
                      -- Если есть одно совпадение и связь по префиксам и постфиксам
                      or (:CNT_MEASURES_SPEED = 1
                          and exists (select null
                                        from D_V_DOSE_MEASURES dm
                                       where dm.ID = :DOSE_MEASURE_ID
                                         and regexp_replace(ms.MNEMOCODE, '/[^/]*$', '') = dm.MNEMOCODE)
                          and regexp_substr(ms.MNEMOCODE, '\/([^\/]+)$', 1, 1, NULL, 1) =
                              case when coalesce(:MEASURE_VAR,
                                                 case when :DURING = '1' then :MEASURE_CTRL
                                                      else null
                                                 end) = 'HOUR' then 'час'
                                   when coalesce(:MEASURE_VAR,
                                                 case when :DURING = '1' then :MEASURE_CTRL
                                                      else null
                                                 end) = 'MIN' then 'мин'
                              end))
                 and exists (select null
                               from D_V_CATALOGS c
                              where c.ID = ms.CID
                                and c.C_UNITCODE = 'MEASURES'
                                and c.C_NAME = 'Скорость введения')

  [6] M2 Action: getMpPrescribesPriorityOption
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare
                    nPRIORITY_OPT NUMBER(17);
                  begin
                    nPRIORITY_OPT := D_PKG_OPTIONS.GET('MpPrescribesPriority', :LPU);
      
                    if nPRIORITY_OPT = 0 then
                      :pnPRIORITY := null;
                    elsif nPRIORITY_OPT = 1 then
                      :pnPRIORITY := NVL(D_PKG_MP_MODEL_PRESC_SP.GET_MAX_PRIORITY(:pnDISEASECASE) + 1, 0);
                    elsif nPRIORITY_OPT = 2 then
                      :pnPRIORITY := NVL(D_PKG_MP_MODEL_PRESC_SP.GET_MIN_PRIORITY(:pnDISEASECASE) - 1, 0);
                    end if;
      
                    if :pnPRIORITY < 1 then
                      :pnPRIORITY := 1;
                    end if;
                  end;
              

      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_MP_MODEL_PRESC_SP.GET_MAX_PRIORITY;
          D_PKG_MP_MODEL_PRESC_SP.GET_MIN_PRIORITY;

  [9] M2 Action: selectAction
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              declare
                nHH_ID NUMBER(17);
                -- Переменные для хранения актуальных данных из номенклатора
                nCurrentDose     D_V_NOMMODIF.DOSE%type;
                nCurrentDosePack D_V_NOMMODIF.DOSE_PACK%type;
                nCurrentKoeff    D_V_NOMMODIF.KOEFF%type;
                nCurrentMnnId    D_V_NOMBASE_MNN.ID%type;
                -- Переменные для хранения старых значений из назначения
                nOldDose         D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES.NOMMODIF_DOSE%type;
                nOldDosePack     D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES.NOMMODIF_DOSE_PACK%type;
                nOldKoeff        D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES.KOEFF%type;
                nOldMnnId        D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES.MNN_ID%type;
              begin
                :DATE_BEGIN := to_char(trunc(sysdate), D_PKG_STD.FRM_D);
                :DATE_CREATE := to_char(trunc(sysdate), D_PKG_STD.FRM_D);
                :SYS_DATE := to_char(trunc(sysdate), D_PKG_STD.FRM_D);
      
                -- Получаем данные из копируемого/редактируемого назначения
                select t.MP_TYPE_CODE,
                       t.NOMMODIF_ID,
                       coalesce((select n.NOM_NAME
                                   from D_V_NOMBASE_BASE n
                                  where exists (select null
                                                  from D_V_NOMMODIF_BASE m
                                                 where m.ID = t.NOMMODIF_ID
                                                   and m.PID = n.ID)), (select nbm.MNN_NAME_RUS
                                                                          from D_V_NOMBASE_MNN nbm
                                                                         where nbm.ID = t.MNN_ID)),
                       t.NOMMODIF_NAME,
                       case when t.MP_CLASS = 4 then D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(t.DOSE)
                         else D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(t.NOMMODIF_DOSE * t.NOMMODIF_DOSE_PACK * t.QUANTITY, 1)
                       end,
                       D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(t.NOMMODIF_DOSE, 1),
                       t.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                       t.DOSE_MEASURE,
                       D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR_WITH_DELIMETER(t.ALT_DOSE, ',', 2),
                       t.ALT_MEASURE_CODE,
                       D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(t.QUANTITY, 1),
                       t.NOMMODIF_MAIN_MEASURE,
                       D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(t.DOSE_QUANT, 1),
                       t.MP_DESCRIBE_ID,
                       t.MP_DESCRIBE_ID,
                       t.MP_DESCRIBE_CODE,
                       (select da.D_NAME
                          from D_V_MP_DESCRIBES_ACTIVE da
                         where da.ID = t.MP_DESCRIBE_ID) as MP_DESCRIBE_NAME,
                       t.MED_USE_METHOD_ID,
                       (select dmu.MUM_NAME
                          from D_V_MED_USE_METHODS dmu
                         where dmu.ID = t.MED_USE_METHOD_ID) as MED_USE_METHOD_CAP,
                       t.MA_ATTRIBUTE_ID,
                       D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(t.DOSE * t.DOSE_QUANT, 1),
                       t.HH_DEP,
                       t.USE_UNTIL_CLOSE,
                       to_char(case when :windowMode = 'EDIT' then t.DATE_BEGIN  else sysdate end, 'DD.MM.YYYY'),
                       case when :windowMode = 'EDIT' then to_char(t.DATE_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_T) else to_char(sysdate, D_PKG_STD.FRM_T) end,
                       to_char(case when :windowMode = 'EDIT' then t.DATE_CREATE else sysdate end, 'DD.MM.YYYY'),
                       to_char(t.DATE_CREATE, 'HH24:MI'),
                       case when :windowMode = 'EDIT' then to_char(t.DATE_END, 'DD.MM.YYYY') end,
                       case when :windowMode = 'EDIT' then to_char(t.DATE_BEGIN,'HH24:MI') else to_char(sysdate,'HH24:MI') end,
                       case when :windowMode = 'EDIT' then to_char(t.DATE_END,'HH24:MI') else '23:59' end,
                       t.PATIENT_ID,
                       t.DISEASECASE,
                       t.IS_PAT_NOMBASE,
                       t.NOMMODIF_DOSE_PACK,
                       t.KOEFF,
                       t.NOMMODIF_ACM_DOSE_MEASURE,
                       (select na.DOSE
                          from D_V_NOMMODIF_ACM_BASE na
                         where na.PID = to_number(:NOMMODIF_ID)),
                       (D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(t.NOMMODIF_ACM_DOSE) * t.NOMMODIF_ACM_DOSE_PACK) / (t.NOMMODIF_DOSE * t.NOMMODIF_DOSE_PACK),
                       case when t.MTS_DESC is not null then t.MTS_DESC else 0 end,
                       t.IS_ONKO,
                       t.DURATION,
                       t.DURATION_MEASURE,
                       t.PRIORITY,
                       t.COMMENTARY,
                       t.MED_USE_METHOD_ID,
                       t.SPEED,
                       (select ms.M_NAME
                          from D_V_MEASURES ms
                         where ms.ID = t.SPEED),
                       t.MP_CLASS,
                       t.MED_FORMS,
                       t.MNN_ID,
                       t.RED_INJ,
                       -- Сохраняем старые значения для сравнения
                       t.NOMMODIF_DOSE,
                       t.NOMMODIF_DOSE_PACK,
                       t.KOEFF,
                       t.MNN_ID
                  into :MP_TYPE,
                       :NOMMODIF_ID,
                       :NOMBASE,
                       :NOMMODIF,
                       :DOSE,
                       :REAL_DOSE,
                       :DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                       :DOSE_MEASURE,
                       :ALT_DOSE,
                       :ALT_MEASURE_CODE,
                       :QUANTITY,
                       :NOMMODIF_MAIN_MEASURE,
                       :DOSE_QUANT,
                       :MP_DESCRIBE_ID,
                       :MP_DESCRIBE_ID_VAR,
                       :MP_DESCRIBE_CODE,
                       :MP_DESCRIBE,
                       :MED_USE_METHOD,
                       :MED_USE_METHOD_CAP,
                       :MP_ADD_ATTR,
                       :AMOUNT,
                       :HH_DEP,
                       :USE_UNTIL_CLOSE,
                       :DATE_BEGIN,
                       :TIME_BEGIN_HAND,
                       :DATE_CREATE,
                       :TIME_CREATE,
                       :DATE_END,
                       :TIME_BEGIN,
                       :TIME_END,
                       :PATIENT_ID,
                       :DISEASECASE,
                       :IS_PAT_MED,
                       :NOMMODIF_DOSE_PACK,
                       :KOEFF,
                       :ACM_DOSE_MEASURE,
                       :ACM_DOSE,
                       :ACM_KOEFF,
                       :MTS_DESC,
                       :ANTITUMOR_DRUG,
                       :DURATION,
                       :MEASURE,
                       :PRIORITY,
                       :COMMENTARY,
                       :USE_METHOD_ID,
                       :SPEED,
                       :SPEED_CAPTION,
                       :MP_CLASS,
                       :MED_FORMS,
                       :MNN_ID,
                       :RED_INJ,
                       -- Сохраняем старые значения в переменные
                       nOldDose,
                       nOldDosePack,
                       nOldKoeff,
                       nOldMnnId
                  from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES t
                 where t.ID = :ID;
      
                -- Инициализируем сообщение об ошибке
                :MESSAGE_ERROR := null;
      
                -- Для режима EDIT проверяем расхождения с текущим номенклатором
                if :windowMode = 'EDIT' then
                  -- Проверка для обычных препаратов (MP_CLASS != 4)
                  if to_number(:MP_CLASS) != 4 and :NOMMODIF_ID is not null then
                    begin
                      select n.DOSE,
                             n.DOSE_PACK,
                             n.KOEFF
                        into nCurrentDose,
                             nCurrentDosePack,
                             nCurrentKoeff
                        from D_V_NOMMODIF n
                       where n.ID = to_number(:NOMMODIF_ID);
      
                      -- Формируем предупреждение, если есть расхождения
                      if nCurrentDose is not null and nCurrentDose != nOldDose then
                        :MESSAGE_ERROR := :MESSAGE_ERROR || 'Дозировка препарата в номенклаторе изменилась с ' || D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nOldDose, 1) || ' на ' || D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nCurrentDose, 1) || '. ';
                      end if;
      
                      if nCurrentDosePack is not null and nCurrentDosePack != nOldDosePack then
                        :MESSAGE_ERROR := :MESSAGE_ERROR || 'Фасовка препарата в номенклаторе изменилась с ' || D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nOldDosePack, 1) || ' на ' || D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nCurrentDosePack, 1) || '. ';
                      end if;
      
                      if nCurrentKoeff is not null and nCurrentKoeff != nOldKoeff then
                        :MESSAGE_ERROR := :MESSAGE_ERROR || 'Коэффициент пересчета в номенклаторе изменился с ' || D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nOldKoeff, 1) || ' на ' || D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nCurrentKoeff, 1) || '. ';
                      end if;
      
                    exception when no_data_found then
                      :MESSAGE_ERROR := 'Препарат не найден в текущем номенклаторе. ';
                    end;
                  end if;
      
                  -- Проверка для МНН препаратов (MP_CLASS = 4)
                  if to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4 and :MNN_ID is not null then
                    begin
                      select mnn.ID
                        into nCurrentMnnId
                        from D_V_NOMBASE_MNN mnn
                       where mnn.ID = to_number(:MNN_ID);
                      -- МНН актуален, ничего не делаем
                    exception when no_data_found then
                      :MESSAGE_ERROR := :MESSAGE_ERROR || ' МНН препарата не найден в текущем справочнике. ';
                    end;
                  end if;
      
                  -- Если есть сообщение, добавляем рекомендацию
                  if :MESSAGE_ERROR is not null then
                    :MESSAGE_ERROR := 'Внимание! ' || :MESSAGE_ERROR ||
                      'Рекомендуется проверить корректность дозировки перед сохранением.';
                  end if;
      
                -- Для режима COPY обновляем данные из номенклатора (как было ранее)
                elsif :windowMode = 'COPY' then
                  if to_number(:MP_CLASS) != 4 and :NOMMODIF_ID is not null then
                    begin
                      select n.DOSE,
                             n.DOSE_PACK,
                             n.KOEFF
                        into nCurrentDose,
                             nCurrentDosePack,
                             nCurrentKoeff
                      from D_V_NOMMODIF n
                     where n.ID = to_number(:NOMMODIF_ID);
      
                      if nCurrentDose is not null then
                        :REAL_DOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nCurrentDose, 1);
                      end if;
      
                      if nCurrentDosePack is not null then
                        :NOMMODIF_DOSE_PACK := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nCurrentDosePack, 1);
                      end if;
      
                      if nCurrentKoeff is not null then
                        :KOEFF := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nCurrentKoeff, 1);
                      end if;
      
                      if :QUANTITY is not null then
                        :DOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(
                          D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:QUANTITY) *
                          nCurrentDose *
                          nCurrentDosePack, 1);
                      end if;
      
                    exception when no_data_found then
                      null;
                    end;
                  end if;
      
                  if to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4 and :MNN_ID is not null then
                    begin
                      select mnn.ID
                        into nCurrentMnnId
                        from D_V_NOMBASE_MNN mnn
                       where mnn.ID = to_number(:MNN_ID);
                    exception when no_data_found then
                      :MNN_ID := null;
                    end;
                  end if;
                end if;
      
                :DOSE_CAPT := 'Дозировка: ' || D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR_WITH_DELIMETER(D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:DOSE), '.', 2) || ' ' || :DOSE_MEASURE;
      
                begin
                  select nd.MED_ID
                    into :MF
                    from D_V_NOMMODIF_BASE nd
                   where nd.ID = to_number(:NOMMODIF_ID);
                exception when no_data_found then
                  :MF := null;
                end;
      
                :FIN_DATE_TYPE := 0;
                --для копирования с предыдущих отделений
                if :windowMode='COPY' then
                  begin
                    select hhd.PID
                      into nHH_ID
                      from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE hhd
                     where hhd.ID = :HH_DEP;
      
                    select dhh.ID
                      into :HH_DEP_FOR_MP
                      from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE dhh
                     where dhh.PID = nHH_ID
                       and dhh.IS_LAST = 1;
                  end;
                else
                  :HH_DEP_FOR_MP := :HH_DEP;
                end if;
      
                :UseAllergenNommodif := D_PKG_OPTION_SPECS.GET(pnLPU => :LPU,psSO_CODE => 'UseAllergenNommodif');
      
                select case when exists(select null
                                          from D_V_MP_DESC_TIMES v
                                         where v.PID = :MP_DESCRIBE_ID) then 2
                            else 1
                        end
                  into :CNT_MP_DESC_TIMES
                  from dual;
      
                select case when exists(select null
                                          from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE hhd
                                               join D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE hh on hh.ID = hhd.PID
                                               join D_V_HPK_PLAN_JOURNALS_BASE hpj on hpj.ID = hh.HPK_PLAN_JOURNAL
                                               join D_V_DIR_THERAPY_SCHEMES dts on dts.PID = hpj.DIRECTION
                                               join D_V_PRESCRIBE_ONK_SCH_BASE posc on posc.THERAPY_SCHEME = dts.THERAPY_SCHEMES_ID
                                               join D_V_PRESCRIBE_ONK_SCH_SP_BASE poss on poss.PID = posc.ID
                                         where hhd.ID = to_number(:HH_DEP)
                                           and poss.MANUAL = 1
                                           and poss.DAY_START is null
                                           and poss.NOMBASE_MNN = to_number(:MNN_ID))
                             and not exists(select null
                                              from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE mps
                                             where mps.PID = to_number(:ID)) then 1
                            else 0
                       end
                  into :IS_MANUAL
                  from dual;
      
                if :IS_MANUAL = 1 then
                  :TIME_BEGIN_HAND := null;
                end if;
      
                begin
                  select pf.AGENT
                    into :AGENT_ID
                    from D_V_PERSMEDCARD_BASE pf
                   where pf.ID = to_number(:PATIENT_ID);
                exception when no_data_found then
                  :AGENT_ID := null;
                end;
      
                begin
                  select to_char(hhd.DATE_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) HHD_DATE_IN,
                         to_char(hhd.DATE_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_T) HHD_TIME_IN,
                         to_char(hhd.DATE_OUT, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT) HHD_DATE_TIME_OUT
                    into :HHD_DATE_IN,
                         :HHD_TIME_IN,
                         :HHD_DATE_TIME_OUT
                    from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE hhd
                   where hhd.ID = to_number(:HH_DEP);
                exception when no_data_found then
                  :HHD_DATE_IN := null;
                  :HHD_TIME_IN := null;
                  :HHD_DATE_TIME_OUT := null;
                end;
      
                if (D_PKG_OPTIONS.GET('CheckHospOnkoPrescribesEdit', to_number(:LPU), 0) = '1') then
                  begin
                    select 1
                      into :SPEC_PRICE_EXIST
                      from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE mps
                     where mps.PID = to_number(:ID)
                       and exists (select null
                                     from D_V_MP_PRESC_SP_PRICES_BASE mpsp
                                    where mpsp.PID = mps.ID
                                      and coalesce(mpsp.DOSE, mpsp.PRICE_UM, mpsp.ENTERED, mpsp.DISCARD_DOSE) is not null)
                       and rownum = 1;
                  exception when no_data_found then :SPEC_PRICE_EXIST := 0;
                  end;
                end if;
      
                if to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4 then
                  :ALT_DOSE := null;
                end if;
              end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES;
          D_V_PRESCRIBE_ONK_SCH_SP_BASE;
          D_V_PERSMEDCARD_BASE;
          D_V_PRESCRIBE_ONK_SCH_BASE;
          D_V_HPK_PLAN_JOURNALS_BASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE;
          D_V_DIR_THERAPY_SCHEMES;
          D_V_NOMMODIF_ACM_BASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE;
          D_V_NOMBASE_BASE;
          D_V_MP_PRESC_SP_PRICES_BASE;
          D_V_MP_DESCRIBES_ACTIVE;
          D_V_MED_USE_METHODS;
          D_V_MP_DESC_TIMES;
          D_V_MEASURES;
          D_V_NOMBASE_MNN;
          D_V_NOMMODIF;
          D_V_NOMMODIF_BASE;
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE;
      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM;
          D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR_WITH_DELIMETER;
          D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR;
СИСТЕМНЫЕ ОПЦИИ:

  - CheckHospOnkoPrescribesEdit
  - MpPrescribesZHNVLPnotice
  - UsePregnancyNommodif
  - UseMKBNomBase

  [10] M2 Action: getDefParams
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              begin
                  if :HH_DEP is not null then
                      SELECT hhd.ID,
                             hhd.PAYMENT_KIND,
                             hh.DISEASECASE,
                             hh.PATIENT,
                             2,
                             null,
                             to_char(hhd.DATE_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D),
                             to_char(hhd.DATE_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_T),
                             to_char(hhd.DATE_OUT, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT)
                        INTO :HH_DEP,
                             :PAYMENT_KIND_ID,
                             :DISEASECASE,
                             :PATIENT_ID,
                             :MP_TYPE,
                             :DATE_END,
                             :HHD_DATE_IN,
                             :HHD_TIME_IN,
                             :HHD_DATE_TIME_OUT
                        FROM D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE hhd
                             join D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE hh on hh.ID = hhd.PID
                       WHERE hhd.ID = :HH_DEP;
                  elsif :DIRECTION_SERVICE is not null then
                      SELECT ds.HH_DEP,
                             coalesce(to_char(hhd.PAYMENT_KIND),D_PKG_DIRECTION_SERVICES.GET_PAYMENT_KIND(:LPU,ds.ID,1,0)),
                             coalesce(ds.DISEASECASE,(select hh.DISEASECASE from D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE hh where hh.ID = hhd.PID)),
                             d.PATIENT,
                             case when :HH_DEP is null then 3 else 2 end,
                             case when :windowMode is null then to_char(coalesce(v.VISIT_DATE, coalesce(ds.REC_DATE, trunc(sysdate))), D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) end,
                             null,
                             null,
                             null
                        INTO :HH_DEP,
                             :PAYMENT_KIND_ID,
                             :DISEASECASE,
                             :PATIENT_ID,
                             :MP_TYPE,
                             :DATE_END,
                             :HHD_DATE_IN,
                             :HHD_TIME_IN,
                             :HHD_DATE_TIME_OUT
                        FROM D_V_DIRECTION_SERVICES_BASE ds
                             join D_V_DIRECTIONS_BASE d on d.ID = ds.PID
                             left join D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE hhd on hhd.ID = ds.HH_DEP
                             left join D_V_VISITS_BASE v on v.PID = ds.ID
                       WHERE ds.ID = :DIRECTION_SERVICE;
                      if :DISEASECASE is null then
                          D_P_EXC('Не задан случай заболевания, сохраните протокол оказания услуги.');
                      end if;
                  else
                      D_P_EXC('Не указано отделение госпитализации/направление на услугу.');
                  end if;
                  --для копирования с предыдущих отделений
                  if :HH_DEP is not null then
                      :HH_DEP_FOR_MP := :HH_DEP;
                  else
                      :HH_DEP_FOR_MP := null;
                  end if;
                  :SYS_DATE := to_char(trunc(sysdate),D_PKG_STD.FRM_D);
                  :UseAllergenNommodif := D_PKG_OPTION_SPECS.GET(pnLPU => :LPU,
                                                             psSO_CODE => 'UseAllergenNommodif');
                  /* Дата создания */
                  :DATE_CREATE := trunc(sysdate);
                  :TIME_CREATE := to_char(sysdate,'HH24:MI');
                  /* Назначить с */
                  :DATE_BEGIN := trunc(sysdate);
                  :TIME_BEGIN := to_char(sysdate,'HH24:MI');
              end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_DIRECTIONS_BASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE;
          D_V_VISITS_BASE;
          D_V_DIRECTION_SERVICES_BASE;
      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_DIRECTION_SERVICES.GET_PAYMENT_KIND;

  - UseMKBNomBase

  [11] M2 Action: getDescrType
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              begin
                select v.D_TYPE
                  into :D_TYPE
                  from D_V_MP_DESCRIBES v
                 where v.ID = :MP_DESCRIBES;
                select case when exists (select null
                                           from D_V_MP_DESC_TIMES v
                                          where v.PID = :MP_DESCRIBES) then 2
                            else 1
                       end
                  into :CNT_MP_DESC_TIMES
                  from dual;
              end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:

          D_V_MP_DESC_TIMES;

  [12] M2 Action: IS_COMPLEX
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              begin
                    select t.IS_COMPLEX
                      into :IS_COMPLEX
                      from D_V_NOMBASE t, D_V_NOMMODIF t1
                     where t1.pid=t.id
                       and t1.id=:NOMMODIF_ID;
              end;

  [13] M2 Action: doEditNazn
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              begin
                D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.MOVE_NEXT(pnDISEASECASE => :DISEASECASE,
                                              pnPRIORITY    => :PRIORITY);
                :MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN := case when to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 1 and to_number(:MNN_ID) is not null then 5 -- Комплексные препараты с MNN
                                        when to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 2 and to_number(:MNN_ID) is not null then 6 -- Экстемпоральные с MNN
                                        when to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4 or (to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 0 and to_number(:MNN_ID) is not null) then 4 -- MNN препараты (класс 4) или обычные с MNN
                                        else to_number(:MP_CLASS) -- Все остальные случаи - сохраняем исходный класс
                                      end;
              end;
              

      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.MOVE_NEXT;
СИСТЕМНЫЕ ОПЦИИ:

  [16] M2 SubAction: MpTimes
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  begin
                    if :MpTime is not null then
                      /* Если добавили время при редактировании окна, то добавляем в цикле с днями в формате "время" */
                      if length(:MpTime) = 5 then
                        :ADD_TIME_HAND := 0;
                        if :DAYS > 0 then
                          for i in 0 .. :DAYS loop
                            if :DAYS = i and :TIME_END_HAND is not null then
                              if :MpTime > :TIME_END_HAND then
                                return;
                              end if;
                            end if;
                            if :MpTime is not null and :MpTime != '00:00' then
                              D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(to_char(to_date(to_char(to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) + i, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) || ' ' || :MpTime, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS), D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS));
                              :ADD_TIME_HAND := 1;
                            end if;
                          end loop;
                        end if;
                        if :ADD_TIME_HAND = 0 then
                          if :MpTime > :TIME_END_HAND then
                            return;
                          end if;
      
                          if :MpTime is not null and :MpTime != '00:00' then
                            D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(to_char(to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' || :MpTime, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS), D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS));
                            :ADD_TIME_HAND := 1;
                          end if;
                        end if;
                        /* Если время из предыдущего назначения, то добавляем его в формате "дата + время + 00" */
                      else
                        if :MpTime is not null and length(:MpTime) > 15 then
                          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(to_char(to_date(:MpTime, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS), D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS));
                        end if;
                      end if;
                    end if;
                  end;
                  

      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS;
          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET;

  [17] M2 SubAction: MpSchedule
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare
                    nDAYS                   NUMBER := to_number(:SCHEDULE_DAYS);
                    dDATE_BEGIN             DATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D);
                    nDOSE                   D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.DOSE%type;
                    nDOSE_QUANT             D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.DOSE_QUANT%type;
                    nALT_DOSE               NUMBER := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT);
                  begin
                    if (:SCH_TIME is null or nDAYS is null) then
                      return;
                    end if;
      
                    if (nDAYS < 0) then
                      nDAYS := 0;
                    end if;
      
                    -- Определяем DOSE в зависимости от MP_CLASS и MNN_ID
                    if to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4 then
                      -- Для МНН препаратов (MP_CLASS = 4) берем из SCHEDULE_DOSE
                      nDOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE);
                      nALT_DOSE := null;
                    else
                      -- Для обычных препаратов
                      if (:MNN_ID is null) then
                        nDOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:DOSE);
                      else
                        nDOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE);
                      end if;
                    end if;
      
                    -- Определяем DOSE_QUANT в зависимости от MP_CLASS
                    if to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4 then
                      -- Для МНН препаратов DOSE_QUANT всегда = 1
                      nDOSE_QUANT := 1;
                    elsif (to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN) = 4 and :SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU is null) then
                      nDOSE_QUANT := 1;
                    else
                      nDOSE_QUANT := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU);
                    end if;
      
                    for i in 0 .. nDAYS
                    loop
                      if (i = nDAYS and to_date(:SCH_TIME, D_PKG_STD.FRM_TS) > to_date(:TIME_END, D_PKG_STD.FRM_TS)) then
                        exit;
                      end if;
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_SCHEDULE_SET(pnDOSE       => nDOSE,
                                                                         pnDOSE_QUANT => nDOSE_QUANT,
                                                                         pnALT_DOSE   => nALT_DOSE,
                                                                         pnPLAN_DATE  => to_char(dDATE_BEGIN + i, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) || ' ' || :SCH_TIME);
                    end loop;
                  end;
                  

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS;

          D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM;
          D_PKG_STD.FRM_TS;
          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_SCHEDULE_SET;
