  [18] M2 SubAction: SELast
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare
                          dFINDATE        DATE;
                          nDOSE_QUANT     NUMBER(10,3);
                          nDOSE           NUMBER(10,3);
                          nMP_CONDITION   NUMBER(1);
                          dDateBegin      DATE;
                          dDateCreate     DATE;
                  begin
                      dDateCreate := to_date(:DATE_CREATE || ' ' || :TIME_CREATE, 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi');
                      if :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '0' then
                          dFINDATE := to_date(coalesce(:DATE_END, :DATE_END_HAND) || ' ' || coalesce(:TIME_END, :TIME_END_HAND), 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi');
                      elsif :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '1' then
                        if :D_TYPE = 1 then
                          dFINDATE := to_date(coalesce(:DATE_BEGIN, :DATE_BEGIN_HAND) || ' 00:00', 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi') + :DAYSCOUNT - 1/24/60/60;
                        elsif :D_TYPE = 2 then
                          dFINDATE := to_date(coalesce(:DATE_BEGIN, :DATE_BEGIN_HAND) || ' 00:00', 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi') + :DAYSCOUNT;
                        else
                          dFINDATE := to_date(coalesce(:DATE_BEGIN, :DATE_BEGIN_HAND) || ' ' || coalesce(:TIME_BEGIN, :TIME_BEGIN_HAND_V), 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi') + :DAYSCOUNT - 1/24/60/60;
                        end if;
                      else
                          begin
                          select t.PLAN_DATE_OUT
                            into dFINDATE
                            from D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE t
                           where t.DISEASECASE = :DISEASECASE
                         and rownum = 1;
                         end;
                        if dFINDATE is null then
                          D_P_EXC('В истории болезни не проставлена планируемая дата выписки. Назначение "До выписки" невозможно.');
                        end if;
                      end if;
                      if :DIRECTION_SERVICE is not null then
                          nMP_CONDITION := 1;
                      else
                          nMP_CONDITION := 0;
                      end if;
                      -- Для MP_CLASS = 4 (МНН препараты) используем специальную логику
                      if to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4 then
                          -- Для МНН препаратов: DOSE из контрола, QUANTITY всегда = 1
                          nDOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:DOSE_EDIT); -- Берем из поля DOSE
                          nDOSE_QUANT := 1; -- Для МНН всегда 1
      
                          -- Если нужно, можно игнорировать QUANTITY для МНН
                          -- или установить в 1
                          :QUANTITY := 1;
                          :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE := null;
                      else
                          -- Для обычных препаратов: используем стандартную логику
                          nDOSE_QUANT := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:DOSE_QUANT);
                          if (:DOSE_QUANT is null) then
                              nDOSE_QUANT := 1;
                          end if;
      
                          -- Берем DOSE из контрола, а если пусто, то из DOSE_EDIT
                          nDOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(coalesce(:DOSE, :DOSE_EDIT));
                          :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(replace(:ALT_MEASURE_DOSE, ' ', ''));
                      end if;
                      if :D_TYPE = 4 then
                        if :TIME_BEGIN_HAND is not null then
                          if :TIME_BEGIN_HAND is null or :TIME_BEGIN_HAND = '00:00:00' then return; end if;
                          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' ||:TIME_BEGIN_HAND);
                          dDateBegin := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND||' '||:TIME_BEGIN_HAND, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT);
                        else
                          dDateBegin := to_date(coalesce(:DATE_BEGIN, :DATE_BEGIN_HAND)||' '||coalesce(:TIME_BEGIN, :TIME_BEGIN_HAND_V), 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi');
                        end if;
                        dFINDATE := to_date(coalesce(:DATE_END_HAND, to_char(to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND) + :DAYS - 1/24/60/60))||' '||coalesce(:TIME_END_HAND,coalesce(:TIME_BEGIN_HAND, :TIME_BEGIN_HAND_V)), D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT);
                      elsif :D_TYPE in (1, 2) then
                        dDateBegin := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' 00:00', 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi');
                      else
                        dDateBegin := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' '||coalesce(:TIME_BEGIN, :TIME_BEGIN_HAND_V), 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi');
                      end if;
      
                      if :MIN_TIME is not null then
                        dDateBegin := to_date(coalesce(:DATE_BEGIN, :DATE_BEGIN_HAND)||' '||:MIN_TIME, 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi');
                      end if;
      
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.GET_ERRORS(pnID                => to_number(:HH_MP_PRESCR_ID),
                                                     pnLPU               => to_number(:LPU),
                                                     pnDISEASECASE       => to_number(:DISEASECASE),
                                                     pnDIRECTION_SERVICE => to_number(:DIRECTION_SERVICE),
                                                     pnMP_TYPE           => to_number(:MP_TYPE),
                                                     pnNOMMODIF          => to_number(:NOMMODIF),
                                                     pnDOSE              => nDOSE,
                                                     pnDOSE_MEASURE      => coalesce(to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE_CMB), to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE)),
                                                     pnDOSE_QUANT        => case when to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN) = 4 then 1
                                                                                 else nDOSE_QUANT
                                                                            end,
                                                     pnMP_DESCRIBE       => to_number(:MP_DESCRIBE),
                                                     pnMED_USE_METHOD    => to_number(:MED_USE_METHOD),
                                                     pdDATE_BEGIN        => dDateBegin,
                                                     pdDATE_END          => dFINDATE,
                                                     pdDATE_CANCEL       => null,
                                                     pdDATE_CREATE       => to_date(:DATE_CREATE, 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi:ss'),
                                                     pnMP_CONDITION      => nMP_CONDITION,
                                                     psCANCEL_REASON     => null,
                                                     psCOMMENTARY        => to_char(:COMMENTARY),
                                                     pnEMPLOYER          => to_number(:EMPLOYER),
                                                     pnMA_ATTRIBUTE      => to_number(:MP_ADD_ATTR),
                                                     pnIS_PAT_NOMBASE    => to_number(:IS_PAT_MED),
                                                     pnQUANTITY          => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(replace(:QUANTITY, ' ', '')),
                                                     pnUSE_UNTIL_CLOSE   => 0,
                                                     pnHH_DEP            => to_number(:HH_DEP),
                                                     pnPATIENT           => to_number(:PATIENT_ID),
                                                     pnHID               => null,
                                                     pnALT_DOSE          => :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE,
                                                     psWARNING           => :WARN); -- psWARNING выходной параметр
      				if :WARN is not null then
      				  return;
      				end if;
      
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.UPD(pnID               => to_number(:HH_MP_PRESCR_ID),
                                              pnLPU              => to_number(:LPU),
                                              pnMP_TYPE          => to_number(:MP_TYPE),
                                              pnNOMMODIF         => to_number(:NOMMODIF),
                                              pnDOSE             => nDOSE,
                                              pnDOSE_MEASURE     => coalesce(to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE_CMB), to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE)),
                                              pnDOSE_QUANT       => case when to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN) = 4 then 1
                                                                         else nDOSE_QUANT
                                                                    end,
                                              pnMP_DESCRIBE      => to_number(:MP_DESCRIBE),
                                              pnMED_USE_METHOD   => to_number(:MED_USE_METHOD),
                                              pdDATE_BEGIN       => dDateBegin,
                                              pdDATE_END         => dFINDATE,
                                              pdDATE_CANCEL      => null,
                                              pdDATE_CREATE      => dDateCreate,
                                              pnMP_CONDITION     => nMP_CONDITION,
                                              psCANCEL_REASON    => null,
                                              psCOMMENTARY       => to_char(:COMMENTARY),
                                              pnEMPLOYER         => to_number(:EMPLOYER),
                                              pnMA_ATTRIBUTE     => to_number(:MP_ADD_ATTR),
                                              pnIS_PAT_NOMBASE   => to_number(:IS_PAT_MED),
                                              pnQUANTITY         => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(replace(:QUANTITY, ' ', '')),
                                              pnUSE_UNTIL_CLOSE  => to_number(:USE_UNTIL_CLOSE),
                                              pnHH_DEP           => to_number(:HH_DEP),
                                              pnIS_RECIPE        => 0,
                                              pnALT_DOSE         => :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE,
                                              pnMTS_DESC         => to_number(:MTS_DESC),
                                              pnIS_ONKO          => to_number(:IS_ONKO),
                                              pnDURATION         => to_number(:DURATION),
                                              psDURATION_MEASURE => to_char(:MEASURE),
                                              pnPRIORITY         => to_number(:PRIORITY),
                                              vAPI_VERSION       => 15,
                                              pnSPEED            => to_number(:SPEED),
                                              pnMED_FORMS        => to_number(:MED_FORMS),
                                              pnMNN              => to_number(:MNN_ID),
                                              pnMP_CLASS         => to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN),
                                              pnRED_INJ          => to_number(:RED_INJ));
                      /* Заполняем MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.RED_INJ с веба */
                      for cur in (select mps.ID,
                                         mps.LPU,
                                         mps.IS_COMPLEX,
                                         mps.DOSE,
                                         mps.DOSE_MEASURE,
                                         mps.DOSE_QUANT,
                                         mps.NOMMODIF,
                                         mps.PLAN_DATE,
                                         mps.NOTE,
                                         mps.QUANTITY,
                                         mps.PART_SER,
                                         mps.ALT_DOSE,
                                         mps.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                         mps.MP_CLASS,
                                         mps.MNN_ID,
                                         mps.MED_FORMS,
                                         mps.GOODSUPPLY,
                                         /* Если экстемпоральное И верхняя галочка выбрана И это спеки основного препарата, ставим галочки */
                                         case when :MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN = 2 and to_number(:RED_INJ) = 1 and mps.NOMMODIF = to_number(:NOMMODIF) then 1
                                              else case when exists (select /*+ cardinality(fn, 1)*/
                                                                            null
                                                                       from table(cast(D_PKG_TOOLS.STR_SEPARATE_TO_IDS(to_char(case when :NOM_COMPLEX is not null then :NOM_COMPLEX
                                                                                                                                    else :NOM_EX
                                                                                                                               end)) as D_CL_ID)) fn
                                                                      where fn.COLUMN_VALUE = mps.NOMMODIF) then 1
                                                        else 0
                                                   end
                                         end RED_INJ_SPEC
                                    from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE mps
                                   where mps.PID = to_number(:HH_MP_PRESCR_ID))
                      loop
                        if cur.MP_CLASS = 4 then
                          cur.ALT_DOSE := null;
                        end if;
                        D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.UPD(pnID               => cur.ID,
                                                     pnLPU              => cur.LPU,
                                                     pnIS_COMPLEX       => cur.IS_COMPLEX,
                                                     pnDOSE             => cur.DOSE,
                                                     pnDOSE_MEASURE     => cur.DOSE_MEASURE,
                                                     pnDOSE_QUANT       => cur.DOSE_QUANT,
                                                     pnNOMMODIF         => cur.NOMMODIF,
                                                     pdPLAN_DATE        => cur.PLAN_DATE,
                                                     psNOTE             => cur.NOTE,
                                                     pnQUANTITY         => cur.QUANTITY,
                                                     psPART_SER         => cur.PART_SER,
                                                     pnALT_DOSE         => cur.ALT_DOSE,
                                                     pnEX_ALT_DOSE      => cur.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                                     pnMP_CLASS         => cur.MP_CLASS,
                                                     pnMNN              => cur.MNN_ID,
                                                     pnMED_FORMS        => cur.MED_FORMS,
                                                     vAPI_VERSION       => 5,
                                                     pnPLAN_GOODSSUPPLY => cur.GOODSUPPLY,
                                                     pnRED_INJ          => cur.RED_INJ_SPEC);
                      end loop;
                      :LAST_ADDED := to_number(:HH_MP_PRESCR_ID);
                      if to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN) != 4 then
                        D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.GET_LIMIT_ERRORS(pnMP_PRESCRIBE => to_number(:HH_MP_PRESCR_ID),
                                                             pnLPU          => to_number(:LPU),
                                                             psWARN         => :WARN);
                      end if;
                  end;

  [20] M2 Action: checkNazn
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              declare
                  nC NUMBER(5);
                  dDateBegin DATE;
                  nopt NUMBER(1);
                  dAP_DATE_B  DATE;
                  nCOUNT_WEEK NUMBER(3);
                  nSO         NUMBER(1);
                  nDD_CODE    NUMBER(1);
                  nCOUNT_MKB  NUMBER;
                  nSO_MKB     NUMBER(1);
              begin
                  :MSG := null;
                  :SERVICE := null;
                  if :D_TYPE = 4 then
                    dDateBegin:=to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND,D_PKG_STD.FRM_D);
                  else
                      dDateBegin:=to_date(:DATE_BEGIN,D_PKG_STD.FRM_D);
                  end if;
                  /*Проверка вхождения в период отделения*/
                  :DEP_CHECK := 1;
                  if :HH_DEP is not null then
                    declare
                      dDATE_BEGIN date;
                      dFINDATE date;
                      dHhDateOut date;
                    begin
                      begin
                          select to_date(t.PLAN_DATE_OUT, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT)
                            into dHhDateOut
                            from D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE t
                           where t.DISEASECASE = :DISEASECASE
                             and rownum = 1;
                       exception when others then null;
                      end;
                      if :D_TYPE = 4 then
                          begin
                              dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' || :TIME_BEGIN_HAND, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT);
                              if :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '0' then
                                  dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_END_HAND || ' ' || :TIME_END_HAND, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT);
                              elsif :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '1' then
                                  dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' || :TIME_BEGIN_HAND, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT) + :DAYS - 1/24/60/60;
                              else
                                  dFINDATE := dHhDateOut;
                                  if dFINDATE is null then D_P_EXC('В истории болезни не проставлена планируемая дата выписки. Назначение "До выписки" невозможно.'); end if;
                              end if;
                          end;
                      else
                          dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' '||:TIME_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT);
                          if :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '0' then
                              dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_END||' '||:TIME_END, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT);
                          elsif :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '1' then
                            if :D_TYPE in (1, 2) then
                              dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' 00:00', D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT);
                              if :D_TYPE = 1 then
                                dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' 00:00', D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT) + :DAYSCOUNT - 1/24/60/60;
                              else
                                dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' 00:00', D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT) + :DAYSCOUNT;
                              end if;
                            else
                              dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' '||:TIME_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT) + :DAYSCOUNT - 1/24/60/60;
                            end if;
                          else
                              dFINDATE := dHhDateOut;
                              if dFINDATE is null then D_P_EXC('В истории болезни не проставлена планируемая дата выписки. Назначение "До выписки" невозможно.'); end if;
                          end if;
                      end if;
                      select count(1)
                        into :DEP_CHECK
                        from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS hhd
                       where hhd.ID = :HH_DEP
                         and D_PKG_DAT_TOOLS.DATE_RANGES_ERROR(fdBEGIN_1 => to_date(hhd.DATE_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT),
                                                               fdEND_1   => to_date(hhd.DATE_OUT, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT),
                                                               fdBEGIN_2 => dDATE_BEGIN,
                                                               fdEND_2   => dFINDATE) in (5, 3);
                    end;
                  end if;
                  nopt := D_PKG_OPTIONS.GET('MpPrescribesZHNVLPnotice', :LPU);
                  if nopt in (1,2) then
                      select count(1)
                        into nC
                        from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES t
                       where t.MP_TYPE_CODE in (1,2)
                         and trunc(t.DATE_BEGIN) <= dDateBegin
                         and coalesce(t.DATE_CANCEL, t.DATE_END) >= dDateBegin
                         and t.DISEASECASE = :DISEASECASE
                         and rownum < 6;
                      if nC >= 4 then
                          :SERVICE := D_PKG_SERVICES.GET_ID_BY_CODE(D_PKG_CONSTANTS.SEARCH_STR('ST_AGREE_MP_SERVICE',:LPU),:LPU);
                          :SERVICE_CODE := D_PKG_CONSTANTS.SEARCH_STR('ST_AGREE_MP_SERVICE',:LPU);
                          if :SERVICE is not null then
                              if nC > 4 then
                                  select count(1) into nC
                                    from D_V_DIRECTION_SERVICES t
                                   where t.LPU = :LPU
                                     and t.SERVICE_ID = :SERVICE
                                     and t.DISEASECASE = :DISEASECASE;
                              else
                                  nC := 0;
                              end if;
                              if nC = 0 then
                                  :MSG := 'При одновременном назначении пяти и более препаратов одному пациенту необходимо согласование. Услуга «Согласование лекарственных назначений»';
                              else
                                  :SERVICE := null;
                              end if;
                          end if;
                      end if;
                  end if;
                  if nopt in (1,3) then
                        select count(1)
                          into nC
                          from D_V_NOMMODIF m
                               join D_V_NOMBASE b on b.ID = m.PID
                               join D_V_NOMBASE_MNN_ACTIVE_BASE nma on nma.PID = b.ID
                               join D_V_MED_ZHNVLP d on d.MNN_ID = nma.MNN
                               join D_V_LPU l on l.ID = to_number(:LPU)
                         where m.ID          = :NOMMODIF
                           and ((D_PKG_OPTION_SPECS.GET('UseMedFormInZHNVLP', :LPU) = '1' and d.MED_FORM_ID = m.MED_ID) or D_PKG_OPTION_SPECS.GET('UseMedFormInZHNVLP', :LPU) = '0')
                           and d.VERSION     = D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(1, :LPU, 'MED_ZHNVLP')
                           and (d.LPUDICT_ID is null or d.LPUDICT_ID = l.LPUDICT_ID)
                           and rownum = 1;
                      if nC != 1 then
                          if :HH_DEP is not null then
                              select count(1) into nC
                                from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS t
                               where t.ID = :HH_DEP
                                 and ';'||D_PKG_CONSTANTS.SEARCH_STR('PK_EXCLUDE_VK_AGREE_MP',:LPU)||';' like '%;'||t.PAYMENT_KIND||';%';
                          end if;
                          if nC != 1 then
                              :SERVICE1 := D_PKG_SERVICES.GET_ID_BY_CODE(D_PKG_CONSTANTS.SEARCH_STR('ST_VK_AGREE_MP_SERVICE',:LPU),:LPU);
                              :SERVICE_CODE1 := D_PKG_CONSTANTS.SEARCH_STR('ST_VK_AGREE_MP_SERVICE',:LPU);
                              if :SERVICE1 is not null then
                                  :MSG1 := 'При назначении препарата, не входящего в перечень ЖНВЛП необходимо согласование врачебной комиссии. Услуга «ВК на согласование лекарственных назначений»';
                              end if;
                          end if;
                      end if;
                  end if;
                  /* #190975 */
                  begin
                    select ap.BEGIN_DATE
                      into dAP_DATE_B
                      from D_V_AGENT_PREGNANCY ap
                      join D_V_PERSMEDCARD_BASE pmc on pmc.AGENT = ap.PID
                     where pmc.ID = :PATIENT_ID
                       and ((ap.END_DATE > :DATE_BEGIN) or (ap.END_DATE is null));
                     exception when no_data_found then
                       dAP_DATE_B := null;
                  end;
      
                  begin
                    select dv.DD_CODE
                      into nDD_CODE
                      from D_V_NOMBASE nb
                      join D_V_NOMMODIF nm on nm.PID = nb.ID
                      join D_V_DIRECTORIES_DATA_VER dv on dv.ID = nb.UP_ID
                     where nm.ID = :NOMMODIF;
                     exception when no_data_found then
                       nDD_CODE := null;
                  end;
                  if dAP_DATE_B is not null and nDD_CODE is not null then
                    begin
                      nCOUNT_WEEK := round(D_PKG_DAT_TOOLS.FULL_UNITS(:DATE_BEGIN, dAP_DATE_B, 'DD')/7, 0);
                      nSO := D_PKG_OPTIONS.GET('UsePregnancyNommodif',:LPU);
                      if (((nDD_CODE = 1) or
                           (nDD_CODE = 2 and nCOUNT_WEEK > 14) or
                           (nDD_CODE = 3 and nCOUNT_WEEK > 28)) and
                             nSO in (1,2)) then :SO_UPN := nSO;
                      else
                        :SO_UPN := null;
                      end if;
                    end;
                  end if;
      
                  /* #190978 */
                  begin
                    nSO_MKB := D_PKG_OPTIONS.GET('UseMKBNomBase',:LPU);
                    select count(1)
                      into nCOUNT_MKB
                      from D_V_NOMBASE nb
                           join D_V_NOMMODIF n on n.PID = nb.ID
                           join D_V_NOMBASE_MKBS nm on nm.PID = nb.ID
                     where n.ID = :NOMMODIF
                    @if (:HH_DEP){
                           and exists (select null
                                         from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DIAGNS hhdiag
                                        where hhdiag.MKB_ID = nm.MKB_ID
                                          and hhdiag.HOSP_DIAGN_TYPE_KIND in (1,2)
                                          and hhdiag.HH_DEP = :HH_DEP)
                    @}
                    @if (:HH_DEP == ''){
                           and exists (select null
                                         from D_V_DISEASECASES d
                                        where d.MKB_ID = nm.MKB_ID
                                          and d.ID = :DISEASECASE)
                    @}
                    ;
                    if nCOUNT_MKB > 0 and nSO_MKB in (1,2) then :SO_MKB := nSO_MKB;
                    else :SO_MKB := null;
                    end if;
                  end;
              end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES;
          D_V_AGENT_PREGNANCY;
          D_V_LPU;
          D_V_PERSMEDCARD_BASE;
          D_V_NOMBASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE;
          D_V_DIRECTORIES_DATA_VER;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DIAGNS;
          D_V_DIRECTION_SERVICES;
          D_V_NOMBASE_MNN_ACTIVE_BASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS;
          D_V_DISEASECASES;

          D_V_MED_ZHNVLP;
          D_V_NOMBASE_MKBS;

          D_PKG_SERVICES.GET_ID_BY_CODE;

                  begin
                    :MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN := case when to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 1 and to_number(:MNN_ID) is not null then 5
                                               when to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 2 and to_number(:MNN_ID) is not null then 6
                                               when to_number(:MP_CLASS) in (0, 4) and to_number(:MNN_ID) is not null then 4
                                               when to_number(:MP_CLASS) in (0, 1, 2, 3, 5) and to_number(:MNN_ID) is null then to_number(:MP_CLASS)
                                          end;
                  end;

  [25] M2 SubAction: MpTimes
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                      begin
                          :ADD_TIME_HAND := 0;
                          if :DAYS > 0 then
                              for i in 0..:DAYS
                              loop
                                  if :DAYS = i and :TIME_END_HAND is not null then
                                      if :MpTime > :TIME_END_HAND then
                                          return;
                                      end if;
                                  end if;
                                  D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(to_char(to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND,'dd.mm.yyyy')+i,'dd.mm.yyyy')||' '||:MpTime||':00');
                                  :ADD_TIME_HAND := 1;
                              end loop;
                          end if;
                          if :ADD_TIME_HAND = 0 then
                              if :MpTime > :TIME_END_HAND then
                                  return;
                              end if;
                              D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND||' '||:MpTime||':00');
                              :ADD_TIME_HAND := 1;
                          end if;
                      end;

  [26] M2 SubAction: MpSchedule
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare
                    nDAYS                   NUMBER := to_number(:SCHEDULE_DAYS);
                    dDATE_BEGIN             DATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D);
                    nDOSE                   D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.DOSE%type;
                    nDOSE_QUANT             D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.DOSE_QUANT%type;
                  begin
                    if (:SCH_TIME is null or nDAYS is null) then
                      return;
                    end if;
      
                    if (nDAYS < 0) then
                      nDAYS := 0;
                    end if;
      
                    -- РАСЧЕТА DOSE
                    if to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4 then
                      -- Для МНН препаратов (MP_CLASS = 4) берем из SCHEDULE_DOSE
                      nDOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE);
                    else
                      -- Для обычных препаратов
                      if (:MNN_ID is null) then
                        nDOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:DOSE);
                      else
                        nDOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE);
                      end if;
                    end if;
      
                    -- РАСЧЕТА DOSE_QUANT
                    if to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4 then
                      -- Для МНН препаратов DOSE_QUANT всегда = 1
                      nDOSE_QUANT := 1;
                    elsif (to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN) = 4 and :SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU is null) then
                      nDOSE_QUANT := 1;
                    else
                      nDOSE_QUANT := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU);
                    end if;
      
                    for i in 0 .. nDAYS
                    loop
                      if (i = nDAYS and to_date(:SCH_TIME, D_PKG_STD.FRM_TS) > to_date(:TIME_END, D_PKG_STD.FRM_TS)) then
                        exit;
                      end if;
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_SCHEDULE_SET(pnDOSE       => nDOSE,
                                                                         pnDOSE_QUANT => nDOSE_QUANT,
                                                                         pnALT_DOSE   => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT),
                                                                         pnPLAN_DATE  => to_char(dDATE_BEGIN + i, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) || ' ' || :SCH_TIME);
                    end loop;
                  end;
                  

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS;
      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM;
          D_PKG_STD.FRM_TS;
          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_SCHEDULE_SET;

  [27] M2 SubAction: SALast
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare
                    nINSERTED      NUMBER(17);
                    dFINDATE       DATE;
                    dFINDATE_HAND  VARCHAR2(16);
                    nDOSE_QUANT    NUMBER(10,3);
                    nDOSE          NUMBER(10,3);
                    nMP_CONDITION  NUMBER(1);
                    nC             NUMBER(5);
                    dDATE_BEGIN    DATE;
                    dDATE_CREATE   DATE;
                    nDAY           NUMBER(10) := to_number(:DAYS);
                    dDATE_BEGIN_SP DATE;
                  begin
                    -- for pg
                    dDATE_CREATE := to_date(to_char(to_date(:DATE_CREATE), 'DD.MM.YYYY') || ' ' ||
                                            to_char(sysdate, 'HH24:MI'),'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI');
                    if :D_TYPE = 4 then
                      begin
                        dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND, 'DD.MM.YYYY');
                        dFINDATE   := null;
                        if :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '0' then
                          if (to_date(:DATE_END_HAND, 'DD.MM.YYYY') >
                              to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND, 'DD.MM.YYYY')) then
                            dFINDATE_HAND := :DATE_END_HAND || ' ' || :TIME_END_HAND;
                          end if;
                        elsif :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '1' then
                          dFINDATE_HAND := to_char(to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' || :TIME_BEGIN_HAND,
                                                           'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI') + :DAYS - 1 / 24 / 60 / 60, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI');
                        else
                          select to_date(to_char(t.PLAN_DATE_OUT, 'DD.MM.YYYY') || ' 23:59:59', D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS)
                            into dFINDATE_HAND
                            from D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE t
                           where t.DISEASECASE = :DISEASECASE
                             and rownum = 1;
                          if dFINDATE_HAND is null then
                            D_P_EXC('В истории болезни не проставлена планируемая дата выписки. Назначение "До выписки" невозможно.');
                          end if;
                        end if;
                      end;
                    else
                      begin
                        dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN || ' ' || :TIME_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT);
      
                        if :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '0' then
                          dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_END || ' ' || :TIME_END, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI');
                        elsif :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '1' then
                          if :D_TYPE in (1, 2) then
                            dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN || ' 00:00', 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI');
                            if :D_TYPE = 1 then
                              dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN || ' 00:00', 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI') + :DAYSCOUNT - 1 / 24 / 60 / 60;
                            else
                              dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN || ' 00:00', 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI') + :DAYSCOUNT;
                            end if;
                          else
                            dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN || ' ' || :TIME_BEGIN, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI') + :DAYSCOUNT - 1 / 24 / 60 / 60;
                          end if;
                        else
                          select to_date(to_char(t.PLAN_DATE_OUT, 'DD.MM.YYYY') || ' 23:59:59', D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS)
                            into dFINDATE
                            from D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE t
                           where t.DISEASECASE = :DISEASECASE
                             and rownum = 1;
                          if dFINDATE is null then
                            D_P_EXC('В истории болезни не проставлена планируемая дата выписки. Назначение "До выписки" невозможно.');
                          end if;
                        end if;
                      end;
                    end if;
                    if :DIRECTION_SERVICE is not null then
                      nMP_CONDITION := 1;
                    else
                      nMP_CONDITION := 0;
                    end if;
                    nDOSE_QUANT := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:DOSE_QUANT);
                    if (to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN) = 4 and :DOSE_QUANT is null) then
                      nDOSE_QUANT := 1;
                    end if;
                    if (to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN)) = 4 then
                      :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE := null;
                    else
                      :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(replace(:ALT_MEASURE_DOSE, ' ', ''));
                    end if;
                    nDOSE       := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(coalesce(:DOSE, :DOSE_EDIT));
                    if :D_TYPE = 4 and :ADD_TIME_HAND is null and (:W_MODE_REAL <> 'COPY' or :W_MODE_REAL is null) then
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' || :TIME_BEGIN_HAND);
                      if dFINDATE_HAND is not null then
                        D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(dFINDATE_HAND);
                      end if;
                    end if;
                    if :W_MODE_REAL = 'COPY' and to_number(:D_TYPE) = 4 then
                      for cur in (select distinct to_char(mps.PLAN_DATE, D_PKG_STD.FRM_T) MP_TIME
                                    from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE mps
                                   where mps.PID = to_number(:HH_MP_PRESCR_ID)
                                   order by MP_TIME) loop
                        if (cur.MP_TIME is null or :DATE_BEGIN_HAND is null or :TIME_END_HAND is null) then
                          return;
                        end if;
                        dDATE_BEGIN_SP := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' || cur.MP_TIME, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS);
                        if dDATE_BEGIN_SP > to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' || :TIME_END_HAND, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS) then
                          return;
                        end if;
                        if nDAY <= 0 then
                          nDAY := 0;
                        end if;
                        for i in 0 .. nDAY loop
                          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(to_char(dDATE_BEGIN_SP + i, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS));
                        end loop;
                      end loop;
                    end if;
      
                    if :ACTION = 'CHECK' then
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.GET_ERRORS(pnID                => null,
                                                     pnLPU               => :LPU,
                                                     pnDISEASECASE       => :DISEASECASE,
                                                     pnDIRECTION_SERVICE => :DIRECTION_SERVICE,
                                                     pnMP_TYPE           => :MP_TYPE,
                                                     pnNOMMODIF          => case when :MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN = 4 then null
                                                                                 else :NOMMODIF
                                                                            end,
                                                     pnDOSE              => nDOSE,
                                                     pnDOSE_MEASURE      => coalesce(to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE_CMB),
                                                                                     to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE)),
                                                     pnDOSE_QUANT        => nDOSE_QUANT,
                                                     pnMP_DESCRIBE       => :MP_DESCRIBE,
                                                     pnMED_USE_METHOD    => :MED_USE_METHOD,
                                                     pdDATE_BEGIN        => dDATE_BEGIN,
                                                     pdDATE_END          => dFINDATE,
                                                     pdDATE_CANCEL       => null,
                                                     pdDATE_CREATE       => :DATE_CREATE,
                                                     pnMP_CONDITION      => nMP_CONDITION,
                                                     psCANCEL_REASON     => null,
                                                     psCOMMENTARY        => :COMMENTARY,
                                                     pnEMPLOYER          => :EMPLOYER,
                                                     pnMA_ATTRIBUTE      => :MP_ADD_ATTR,
                                                     pnIS_PAT_NOMBASE    => :IS_PAT_MED,
                                                     pnQUANTITY          => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(replace(:QUANTITY, ' ', '')),
                                                     pnUSE_UNTIL_CLOSE   => 0,
                                                     pnHH_DEP            => :HH_DEP,
                                                     pnPATIENT           => :PATIENT_ID,
                                                     pnHID               => null,
                                                     pnALT_DOSE          => :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE,
                                                     psWARNING           => :WARN);
                      if :WARN is not null then
                        return;
                      end if;
                    end if;
      
                    D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.MOVE_NEXT(pnDISEASECASE => :DISEASECASE,
                                                  pnPRIORITY    => :PRIORITY);
      
                    D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.ADD(pnD_INSERT_ID       => nINSERTED,
                                            pnLPU               => :LPU,
                                            pnDISEASECASE       => :DISEASECASE,
                                            pnDIRECTION_SERVICE => :DIRECTION_SERVICE,
                                            pnMP_TYPE           => :MP_TYPE,
                                            pnNOMMODIF          => case when :MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN = 4 then null
                                                                        else :NOMMODIF
                                                                   end,
                                            pnDOSE              => nDOSE,
                                            pnDOSE_MEASURE      => coalesce(to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE_CMB),
                                                                            to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE)),
                                            pnDOSE_QUANT        => nDOSE_QUANT,
                                            pnMP_DESCRIBE       => :MP_DESCRIBE,
                                            pnMED_USE_METHOD    => :MED_USE_METHOD,
                                            pdDATE_BEGIN        => dDATE_BEGIN,
                                            pdDATE_END          => dFINDATE,
                                            pdDATE_CANCEL       => null,
                                            pdDATE_CREATE       => dDATE_CREATE,
                                            pnMP_CONDITION      => nMP_CONDITION,
                                            psCANCEL_REASON     => null,
                                            psCOMMENTARY        => :COMMENTARY,
                                            pnEMPLOYER          => :EMPLOYER,
                                            pnMA_ATTRIBUTE      => :MP_ADD_ATTR,
                                            pnIS_PAT_NOMBASE    => :IS_PAT_MED,
                                            pnQUANTITY          => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(replace(:QUANTITY, ' ', '')),
                                            pnUSE_UNTIL_CLOSE   => 0,
                                            pnHH_DEP            => :HH_DEP,
                                            pnPATIENT           => :PATIENT_ID,
                                            pnALT_DOSE          => :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE,
                                            pnMTS_DESC          => :MTS_DESC,
                                            pnIS_ONKO           => :IS_ONKO,
                                            pnDURATION          => to_number(:DURATION),
                                            psDURATION_MEASURE  => :MEASURE,
                                            pnPRIORITY          => :PRIORITY,
                                            pnMP_PRESCR_ID_SRC  => case when to_number(:D_TYPE) in (4, 6) and :W_MODE_REAL = 'EDIT' then null
                                                                        else to_number(:HH_MP_PRESCR_ID)
                                                                   end,
                                            pnMP_CLASS          => :MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN,
                                            pnSPEED             => case when to_number(:DURATION) = 1 then
                                                                     to_number(:SPEED)
                                                                   end,
                                            pnMNN               => to_number(:MNN_ID),
                                            pnMED_FORMS         => to_number(:MED_FORMS),
                                            pnRED_INJ           => to_number(:RED_INJ));
                    for cur in (select mps.ID,
                                       mps.LPU,
                                       mps.IS_COMPLEX,
                                       mps.DOSE,
                                       mps.DOSE_MEASURE,
                                       mps.DOSE_QUANT,
                                       mps.NOMMODIF,
                                       mps.PLAN_DATE,
                                       mps.NOTE,
                                       mps.QUANTITY,
                                       mps.PART_SER,
                                       mps.ALT_DOSE,
                                       mps.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                       mps.MP_CLASS,
                                       case when :MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN = 2 and to_number(:RED_INJ) = 1 and mps.NOMMODIF = to_number(:NOMMODIF) then 1
                                            else case when exists (select /*+ cardinality(fn, 1)*/
                                                                          null
                                                                     from table(cast(D_PKG_TOOLS.STR_SEPARATE_TO_IDS(to_char(case when :NOM_COMPLEX is not null then :NOM_COMPLEX
                                                                                                                                  else :NOM_EX
                                                                                                                             end)) as D_CL_ID)) fn
                                                                    where fn.COLUMN_VALUE = mps.NOMMODIF) then 1
                                                      else 0
                                                 end
                                       end RED_INJ_SPEC
                                  from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE mps
                                 where mps.PID = nINSERTED)
                    loop
      			    if to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN) = 4 then
      				  cur.ALT_DOSE := null;
      			    end if;
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.UPD(pnID               => cur.ID,
                                                   pnLPU              => cur.LPU,
                                                   pnIS_COMPLEX       => cur.IS_COMPLEX,
                                                   pnDOSE             => cur.DOSE,
                                                   pnDOSE_MEASURE     => cur.DOSE_MEASURE,
                                                   pnDOSE_QUANT       => cur.DOSE_QUANT,
                                                   pnNOMMODIF         => cur.NOMMODIF,
                                                   pdPLAN_DATE        => cur.PLAN_DATE,
                                                   psNOTE             => cur.NOTE,
                                                   pnQUANTITY         => cur.QUANTITY,
                                                   psPART_SER         => cur.PART_SER,
                                                   pnALT_DOSE         => cur.ALT_DOSE,
                                                   pnEX_ALT_DOSE      => cur.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                                   pnMP_CLASS         => cur.MP_CLASS,
                                                   pnMNN              => to_number(:MNN_ID),
                                                   pnMED_FORMS        => to_number(:MED_FORMS),
                                                   vAPI_VERSION       => 5,
                                                   pnPLAN_GOODSSUPPLY => case when to_number(:GS_ID_NEW) is not null and :MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN = 4 then to_number(:GS_ID_NEW)
                                                                              when to_number(:GS_ID) is not null and :MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN = 4 then to_number(:GS_ID)
                                                                         end,
                                                                         /* Если есть текущий NOMMODIF в коллекции NOM_COMPLEX или NOM_EX, то он нажат и пишем 1 */
                                                   pnRED_INJ          => cur.RED_INJ_SPEC);
                    end loop;
                    if to_number(:D_TYPE) = 2 and :HHD_DATE_IN is not null then
                      -- для условно-временной периодичности выставляем для 1 спеки дату по условиям из ЧТЗ
                      for specs in (select mps.ID,
                                           mps.LPU,
                                           mps.IS_COMPLEX,
                                           mps.DOSE,
                                           mps.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                                           mps.DOSE_QUANT,
                                           mps.NOMMODIF_ID,
                                           mps.NOTE,
                                           mps.QUANTITY,
                                           mps.PART_SER,
                                           mps.ALT_DOSE,
                                           mps.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                           mps.MP_CLASS
                                      from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS mps
                                     where mps.PID = nINSERTED
                                       and trunc(mps.PLAN_DATE) =
                                           (select min(trunc(mps_in.PLAN_DATE))
                                              from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE mps_in
                                             where mps_in.PID = nINSERTED))
                      loop
                        if specs.MP_CLASS = 4 then
                          specs.ALT_DOSE := null;
                        end if;
                        D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.UPD(pnID               => specs.ID,
                                                     pnLPU              => specs.LPU,
                                                     pnIS_COMPLEX       => specs.IS_COMPLEX,
                                                     pnDOSE             => specs.DOSE,
                                                     pnDOSE_MEASURE     => specs.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                                                     pnDOSE_QUANT       => specs.DOSE_QUANT,
                                                     pnNOMMODIF         => specs.NOMMODIF_ID,
                                                     pdPLAN_DATE        => case when to_date(:HHD_DATE_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) = to_date(:DATE_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D)
                                                                                 and to_date(:HHD_TIME_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_T) <= to_date(:TIME_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_T)
                                                                                  then to_date(:HHD_DATE_IN || ' ' || :HHD_TIME_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT)
                                                                                when to_date(:HHD_DATE_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) < to_date(:DATE_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D)
                                                                                  then trunc(dDATE_BEGIN)
                                                                           end,
                                                     psNOTE             => specs.NOTE,
                                                     pnQUANTITY         => specs.QUANTITY,
                                                     psPART_SER         => specs.PART_SER,
                                                     pnALT_DOSE         => specs.ALT_DOSE,
                                                     pnEX_ALT_DOSE      => specs.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                                     pnMP_CLASS         => specs.MP_CLASS,
                                                     pnMNN              => to_number(:MNN_ID),
                                                     pnMED_FORMS        => to_number(:MED_FORMS),
                                                     vAPI_VERSION       => 4,
                                                     pnPLAN_GOODSSUPPLY => case when to_number(:GS_ID_NEW) is not null and to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN) = 4 then to_number(:GS_ID_NEW)
                                                                                when to_number(:GS_ID) is not null and to_number(:MP_CLASS_FROM_MNN) = 4 then to_number(:GS_ID)
                                                                           end);
                      end loop;
                    end if;
                    select count(1)
                      into nC
                      from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE
                     where PID = nINSERTED;
                    if nC = 0 then
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.DEL(nINSERTED, :LPU);
                    else
                      if :F_STR is null then
                        :FULL_STR := nINSERTED;
                      else
                        :FULL_STR := :F_STR || ';' || nINSERTED;
                      end if;
                    end if;
                    :LAST_ADDED := nINSERTED;
                    if nC <> 0 and to_number(:MNN_ID) is null then
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.GET_LIMIT_ERRORS(nINSERTED, :LPU, :WARN);
                    end if;
                    if to_number(:DEL_MP_PRESC) = 1 and :W_MODE_REAL = 'EDIT' then
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.DEL(:HH_MP_PRESCR_ID, :LPU);
                    end if;
                  end;
                  

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE;
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE;
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS;

                  declare nIS_EXECUTED number(1);
                  begin
                      for cur in (select ID,
                                         IS_EXECUTED
                                    from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS
                                   where instr(';'||:IDD||';',';'||ID||';') != 0) loop
                          if cur.IS_EXECUTED = 1 then
                              D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.PRESCRIBE_CANCEL_EXECUTION(pnID  => cur.ID,
                                                                                  pnLPU => to_number(:LPU));
                          end if;
                          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.DEL(pnID  => cur.ID,
                                                       pnLPU => to_number(:LPU));
                      end loop;
                  end;

  [32] M2 SubAction: MpTimes
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare
                    dDATE_BEGIN DATE;
                    nDAY        NUMBER(10) := to_number(:DAYS);
                  begin
                    :ADD_TIME_HAND := '0';
                    if (:MPTIME is null or :DATE_BEGIN_HAND is null or :TIME_END_HAND is null) then
                      return;
                    end if;
                    dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' || :MPTIME, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS);
                    if dDATE_BEGIN > to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND || ' ' || :TIME_END_HAND, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS) then
                      return;
                    end if;
                    if nDAY > 0 then
                      for i in 0 .. nDAY
                      loop
                        D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(to_char(dDATE_BEGIN + i, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS));
                      end loop;
                      :ADD_TIME_HAND := '1';
                    end if;
                    if :ADD_TIME_HAND = '0' then
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET(to_char(dDATE_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS));
                    end if;
                  end;
                  

      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS;
          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_DATETIME_SET;

  [33] M2 SubAction: MpSchedule
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare
                    nDAYS                 NUMBER := to_number(:SCHEDULE_DAYS);
                    dDATE_BEGIN           DATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D);
                  begin
                    if (:SCHEDULE_TIME is null or nDAYS is null) then
                      return;
                    end if;
      
                    if (nDAYS < 0) then
                      nDAYS := 0;
                    end if;
      
                    for i in 0 .. nDAYS
                    loop
                      if (i = nDAYS and to_date(:SCHEDULE_TIME, D_PKG_STD.FRM_TS) > to_date(:TIME_END, D_PKG_STD.FRM_TS)) then
                        exit;
                      end if;
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_SCHEDULE_SET(pnDOSE       => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:DOSE),
                                                                         pnDOSE_QUANT => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU),
                                                                         pnALT_DOSE   => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT),
                                                                         pnPLAN_DATE  => to_char(dDATE_BEGIN + i, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) || ' ' || :SCHEDULE_TIME);
                    end loop;
                  end;
                  

      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM;
          D_PKG_STD.FRM_TS;
          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.CREATE_SPECS_SCHEDULE_SET;

  [34] M2 SubAction: SALastSave
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare nINSERTED   NUMBER(17);
                          dFINDATE    DATE;
                          nC          NUMBER(5) := 0;
                          dDATE_BEGIN DATE;
                          dDateCreate DATE;
                          nMP_CLASS   NUMBER(2);
                  begin
      			    -- for pg
                      dDateCreate:=to_date(to_char(to_date(:DATE_CREATE), 'dd.mm.yyyy')||' '||to_char(sysdate, 'hh24:mi'), 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi');
                      if :D_TYPE=4 then
                          begin
                              dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN_HAND,'dd.mm.yyyy');
                              dFINDATE := null;
                          end;
                      else
                          begin
                              dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN || ' ' || :TIME_BEGIN, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI');
                              if :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '0' then
                                  dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_END||' '||:TIME_END, 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi');
                              elsif :FIN_DATE_TYPE = '1' then
                                if :D_TYPE in (1, 2) then
                                  dDATE_BEGIN := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' 00:00', 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi');
                                  if :D_TYPE = 1 then
                                    dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' 00:00', 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi') + :DAYSCOUNT - 1/24/60/60;
                                  else
                                    dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' 00:00', 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi') + :DAYSCOUNT;
                                  end if;
                                else
                                  dFINDATE := to_date(:DATE_BEGIN||' '||:TIME_BEGIN, 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi') + :DAYSCOUNT - 1/24/60/60;
                                end if;
                              else
                                   select to_date(to_char(t.PLAN_DATE_OUT, 'DD.MM.YYYY') || ' 23:59:59', D_PKG_STD.FRM_DTS)
                                     into dFINDATE
                                     from D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE t
                                    where t.DISEASECASE = :DISEASECASE
                                      and rownum = 1;
                                  if dFINDATE is null then
                                      D_P_EXC('В истории болезни не проставлена планируемая дата выписки. Назначение "До выписки" невозможно.');
                                  end if;
                              end if;
                          end;
                      end if;
      
                      if :CREATE_PRESCRIBES_ONLY = 1 then
                          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.gnMASS_RESTRICT_AUTO_EXECUTION := 1;
                      end if;
      
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.MOVE_NEXT(pnDISEASECASE => :DISEASECASE,
                                                    pnPRIORITY    => :PRIORITY);
                      nMP_CLASS := case when to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 1 and to_number(:MNN_ID) is not null then 5
                                        when to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 2 and to_number(:MNN_ID) is not null then 6
                                        when to_number(:MP_CLASS) in (0, 4) and to_number(:MNN_ID) is not null then 4
                                        when to_number(:MP_CLASS) in (0, 1, 2, 3, 5) and to_number(:MNN_ID) is null then to_number(:MP_CLASS)
                                   end;
                      if (to_number(:MP_CLASS) = 4) then
                        :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE := null;
                      else
                        :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE := D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(replace(:ALT_MEASURE_DOSE, ' ', ''));
                      end if;
                      D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.ADD(pnD_INSERT_ID       => nINSERTED,
                                              pnLPU               => :LPU,
                                              pnDISEASECASE       => :DISEASECASE,
                                              pnDIRECTION_SERVICE => :DIRECTION_SERVICE,
                                              pnMP_TYPE           => :MP_TYPE,
                                              pnNOMMODIF          => case when nMP_CLASS = 4 then null
                                                                          else :NOMMODIF
                                                                     end,
                                              pnDOSE              => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:DOSE),
                                              pnDOSE_MEASURE      => coalesce(to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE_CMB), to_number(:DOSE_MEASURE)),
                                              pnDOSE_QUANT        => case when nMP_CLASS = 4 then 1
                                                                          else D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(:DOSE_QUANT)
                                                                     end,
                                              pnMP_DESCRIBE       => :MP_DESCRIBE,
                                              pnMED_USE_METHOD    => :MED_USE_METHOD,
                                              pdDATE_BEGIN        => dDATE_BEGIN,
                                              pdDATE_END          => dFINDATE,
                                              pdDATE_CANCEL       => null,
                                              pdDATE_CREATE       => dDateCreate,
                                              pnMP_CONDITION      => 1,
                                              psCANCEL_REASON     => null,
                                              psCOMMENTARY        => :COMMENTARY,
                                              pnEMPLOYER          => :EMPLOYER,
                                              pnMA_ATTRIBUTE      => :MP_ADD_ATTR,
                                              pnIS_PAT_NOMBASE    => 0,
                                              pnQUANTITY          => D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM(replace(:QUANTITY, ' ', '')),
                                              pnUSE_UNTIL_CLOSE   => 0,
                                              pnHH_DEP            => :HH_DEP,
                                              pnPATIENT           => :PATIENT_ID,
                                              pnALT_DOSE          => :ALT_MEASURE_DOSE,
                                              pnMTS_DESC          => :MTS_DESC,
                                              pnIS_ONKO           => :IS_ONKO,
                                              pnDURATION          => :DURATION,
                                              psDURATION_MEASURE  => :MEASURE,
                                              pnPRIORITY          => :PRIORITY,
                                              pnMP_CLASS          => nMP_CLASS,
                                              pnSPEED             => case when :DURATION = 1 then :SPEED end,
                                              pnMNN               => to_number(:MNN_ID),
                                              pnMED_FORMS         => to_number(:MED_FORMS),
                                              pnRED_INJ           => to_number(:RED_INJ));
      
                    if :CREATE_PRESCRIBES_ONLY = 1 then
                      null;
                    else
      
                    if to_number(:D_TYPE) = 2 and :HHD_DATE_IN is not null then
                      -- для условно-временной периодичности выставляем для 1 спеки дату по условиям из ЧТЗ
                      for specs in (select mps.ID,
                                           mps.LPU,
                                           mps.IS_COMPLEX,
                                           mps.DOSE,
                                           mps.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                                           mps.DOSE_QUANT,
                                           mps.NOMMODIF_ID,
                                           mps.NOTE,
                                           mps.QUANTITY,
                                           mps.PART_SER,
                                           mps.ALT_DOSE,
                                           mps.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                           mps.MP_CLASS
                                      from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS mps
                                     where mps.PID = nINSERTED
                                       and trunc(mps.PLAN_DATE) =
                                           (select min(trunc(mps_in.PLAN_DATE))
                                              from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE mps_in
                                             where mps_in.PID = nINSERTED))
                      loop
                        if specs.MP_CLASS = 4 then
                          specs.ALT_DOSE := null;
                        end if;
                        D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.UPD(pnID               => specs.ID,
                                                     pnLPU              => specs.LPU,
                                                     pnIS_COMPLEX       => specs.IS_COMPLEX,
                                                     pnDOSE             => specs.DOSE,
                                                     pnDOSE_MEASURE     => specs.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                                                     pnDOSE_QUANT       => specs.DOSE_QUANT,
                                                     pnNOMMODIF         => specs.NOMMODIF_ID,
                                                     pdPLAN_DATE        => case when to_date(:HHD_DATE_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) = to_date(:DATE_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D)
                                                                                 and to_date(:HHD_TIME_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_T) <= to_date(:TIME_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_T)
                                                                                  then to_date(:HHD_DATE_IN || ' ' || :HHD_TIME_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_DT)
                                                                                when to_date(:HHD_DATE_IN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D) < to_date(:DATE_BEGIN, D_PKG_STD.FRM_D)
                                                                                  then trunc(dDATE_BEGIN)
                                                                           end,
                                                     psNOTE             => specs.NOTE,
                                                     pnQUANTITY         => specs.QUANTITY,
                                                     psPART_SER         => specs.PART_SER,
                                                     pnALT_DOSE         => specs.ALT_DOSE,
                                                     pnEX_ALT_DOSE      => specs.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                                     pnMP_CLASS         => specs.MP_CLASS,
                                                     pnMNN              => to_number(:MNN_ID),
                                                     pnMED_FORMS        => to_number(:MED_FORMS),
                                                     vAPI_VERSION       => 4,
                                                     pnPLAN_GOODSSUPPLY => case when to_number(:GS_ID_NEW) is not null and to_number(nMP_CLASS) = 4 then to_number(:GS_ID_NEW)
                                                                                when to_number(:GS_ID) is not null and to_number(nMP_CLASS) = 4 then to_number(:GS_ID)
                                                                           end);
                      end loop;
                    end if;
      
                          for cur in (select mps.ID,
                                             mps.LPU,
                                             mps.PID,
                                             mps.IS_COMPLEX,
                                             mps.DOSE,
                                             mps.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                                             mps.DOSE_MEASURE,
                                             mps.DOSE_QUANT,
                                             mps.NOMMODIF_ID,
                                             mps.NOMMODIF_CODE,
                                             mps.NOMMODIF_NAME,
                                             mps.NOMODIF_LIFE,
                                             mps.PLAN_DATE,
                                             mps.IS_EXECUTED,
                                             mps.EX_DOSE,
                                             mps.EX_DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                                             mps.EX_DOSE_MEASURE,
                                             mps.EX_DOSE_QUANT,
                                             mps.EX_NOMMODIF_ID,
                                             mps.EX_NOMMODIF_CODE,
                                             mps.EX_NOMMODIF_NAME,
                                             mps.EX_DATE,
                                             mps.NOTE,
                                             mps.QUANTITY,
                                             mps.PART_SER,
                                             mps.ALT_DOSE,
                                             mps.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                             mps.MP_CLASS,
                                             case when exists (select /*+ cardinality(fn, 1)*/
                                                                      null
                                                                 from table(cast(D_PKG_TOOLS.STR_SEPARATE_TO_IDS(to_char(:NOM_COMPLEX)) as D_CL_ID)) fn
                                                                where fn.COLUMN_VALUE = mps.NOMMODIF_ID) and :NOM_COMPLEX is not null then 1
                                                  when exists (select /*+ cardinality(fn, 1)*/
                                                                      null
                                                                 from table(cast(D_PKG_TOOLS.STR_SEPARATE_TO_IDS(to_char(:NOM_EX)) as D_CL_ID)) fn
                                                                where fn.COLUMN_VALUE = mps.NOMMODIF_ID) and :NOM_EX is not null then 1
                                                  else 0
                                             end RED_INJ_SPEC
                                        from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS mps
                                       where mps.PID = nINSERTED)
                          loop
                            nC := nC + 1;
                            if cur.MP_CLASS = 4 then
                              cur.ALT_DOSE := null;
                            end if;
                            D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.UPD(pnID               => cur.ID,
                                                         pnLPU              => cur.LPU,
                                                         pnIS_COMPLEX       => cur.IS_COMPLEX,
                                                         pnDOSE             => cur.DOSE,
                                                         pnDOSE_MEASURE     => cur.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                                                         pnDOSE_QUANT       => cur.DOSE_QUANT,
                                                         pnNOMMODIF         => cur.NOMMODIF_ID,
                                                         pdPLAN_DATE        => cur.PLAN_DATE,
                                                         psNOTE             => cur.NOTE,
                                                         pnQUANTITY         => cur.QUANTITY,
                                                         psPART_SER         => cur.PART_SER,
                                                         pnALT_DOSE         => cur.ALT_DOSE,
                                                         pnEX_ALT_DOSE      => cur.EX_ALT_DOSE,
                                                         pnMP_CLASS         => cur.MP_CLASS,
                                                         pnMNN              => to_number(:MNN_ID),
                                                         pnMED_FORMS        => to_number(:MED_FORMS),
                                                         vAPI_VERSION       => 5,
                                                         pnPLAN_GOODSSUPPLY => case when to_number(:GS_ID_NEW) is not null and nMP_CLASS = 4 then to_number(:GS_ID_NEW)
                                                                                    when to_number(:GS_ID) is not null and nMP_CLASS = 4 then to_number(:GS_ID)
                                                                               end,
                                                         pnRED_INJ          => cur.RED_INJ_SPEC);
                            if cur.IS_EXECUTED = 0 then
                              D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.PRESCRIBE_EXECUTION(pnID              => cur.ID,
                                                                           pnLPU             => to_number(:LPU),
                                                                           pnEX_DOSE         => cur.DOSE,
                                                                           pnEX_DOSE_MEASURE => cur.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                                                                           pnEX_DOSE_QUANT   => cur.DOSE_QUANT,
                                                                           pnEX_NOMMODIF     => cur.NOMMODIF_ID,
                                                                           pnEX_QUANTITY     => null,
                                                                           pdEX_DATE         => coalesce(cur.PLAN_DATE, dDATE_BEGIN),
                                                                           pnEX_EMPLOYER     => to_number(:EMPLOYER),
                                                                           psNOTE            => null);
                            end if;
                            D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.PROCESS_STORE(pnID         => cur.ID,
                                                                   pnLPU        => to_number(:LPU),
                                                                   pnGOODSUPPLY => to_number(:GOODSUPPLY_ID));
                          end loop;
      
      
                      if nC = 0 then
                          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBES.DEL(nINSERTED,:LPU);
                      else
                          if :F_STR is null then
                          :FULL_STR := nINSERTED;
                          else
                          :FULL_STR := :F_STR||';'||nINSERTED;
                          end if;
                      end if;
                    end if;
                  end;
                  

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE;
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS_BASE;
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS;
      Пакеты/функции:

          D_PKG_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS.PROCESS_STORE;
          D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.STR_TO_NUM;

  [37] M2 Action: getIsOnkoMnn
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm

              begin

                  into :IS_ONKO_MNN
