  [38] M2 Action: deleteMpPrescribe
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  declare
                    sCHECK_SH_IN_HH_DEP varchar2(1);
                    nAGES number(5);
                    nMKB_FIELD_ID D_V_VISIT_CON_FIELDS.ID%type;
                    nIN_RANGE_C00_C80 number(1);
                    nIN_RANGE_C97_D09 number(1);
                    nIN_RANGE_C00_D09 number(1);
                    nIN_RANGE_D45_D47 number(1);
                    sVIS_MKB D_V_MKB10_BASE.MKB_CODE%type;
                    sDEP_MKB D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DIAGNS.MKB%type;
                    sCLINIC_MKB D_V_MKB10_BASE.MKB_CODE%type;
                    sRECEIVE_MKB D_V_MKB10_BASE.MKB_CODE%type;
                    nHH_ID number(17);
                  begin
                    sCHECK_SH_IN_HH_DEP := D_PKG_OPTIONS.GET('CheckShInHHDep', :LPU, 0);
      
                    if :HH_ID is null then
                      begin
                        select hhd.PID
                          into nHH_ID
                          from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS hhd
                         where hhd.ID = :HH_DEP;
                      exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then nHH_ID := null;
                      end;
                    end if;
      
                    if :VIS_ID is not null then
                        begin
                          select mkb.MKB_CODE
                            into sVIS_MKB
                            from D_V_VIS_DIAGNOSISES_BASE vd
                            join D_V_MKB10_BASE mkb on mkb.ID = vd.MKB
                           where vd.PID = :VIS_ID
                             and vd.IS_MAIN = 0
                             and rownum = 1;
                        exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then sVIS_MKB := null;
                        end;
                    elsif :DIAGNOZ is not null then
                        begin
                            select mkb.MKB_CODE
                              into sVIS_MKB
                              from D_V_MKB10_BASE mkb
                             where mkb.ID = :DIAGNOZ;
                        exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then sVIS_MKB := null;
                        end;
                    end if;
      
                    begin
                      select case
                               when a.BIRTHDATE is not null and hh.DATE_IN is not null then
                                 D_PKG_DAT_TOOLS.FULL_YEARS(hh.DATE_IN, a.BIRTHDATE)
                               else null
                             end,
                             (select r.MKB
                                from (select hhdia.MKB,
                                             row_number() over (partition by hhdia.HH_DEP order by hhdia.HOSP_DIAGN_TYPE_ID asc nulls last) as RN
                                        from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE hhd
                                        join D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DIAGNS hhdia on hhdia.HH_DEP = hhd.ID
                                       where hhdia.HOSP_DIAGN_TYPE_ID in (0, 5)
                                         and hhd.PID = coalesce(:HH_ID, to_char(nHH_ID))
                                         and (hhd.ID = :HH_DEP or :HH_DEP is null and hhd.IS_LAST = 1)
                                     ) r
                              where r.RN = 1
                             ),
                             mkb1.MKB_CODE,
                             mkb2.MKB_CODE
                        into nAGES,
                             sDEP_MKB,
                             sCLINIC_MKB,
                             sRECEIVE_MKB
                        from D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE hh
                        join D_V_PERSMEDCARD_BASE pmc on pmc.ID = hh.PATIENT
                        join D_V_AGENTS_BASE a on a.ID = pmc.AGENT
                   left join D_V_MKB10_BASE mkb1 on mkb1.ID = hh.MKB_CLINIC
                   left join D_V_MKB10_BASE mkb2 on mkb2.ID = hh.MKB_RECEIVE
                       where hh.ID = coalesce(:HH_ID, to_char(nHH_ID));
                    exception when NO_DATA_FOUND then nAGES := null;
                    end;
      
                    :MKB_CODE := coalesce(sVIS_MKB, sDEP_MKB, sCLINIC_MKB, sRECEIVE_MKB);
                    nIN_RANGE_C00_C80 := D_PKG_MKB10.CHECK_CODE_IN_RANGE(:MKB_CODE, 'C00', 'C80', 1);
                    nIN_RANGE_C97_D09 := D_PKG_MKB10.CHECK_CODE_IN_RANGE(:MKB_CODE, 'C97', 'D09', 1);
                    nIN_RANGE_C00_D09 := D_PKG_MKB10.CHECK_CODE_IN_RANGE(:MKB_CODE, 'C00', 'D09', 1);
                    nIN_RANGE_D45_D47 := D_PKG_MKB10.CHECK_CODE_IN_RANGE(:MKB_CODE, 'D45', 'D47', 1);
      
                    if (sCHECK_SH_IN_HH_DEP = '1') then
                      if ((nAGES is not null and nAGES >= 18) and (nIN_RANGE_C00_C80 = 1 or nIN_RANGE_C97_D09 = 1)) then
                        :REQUIRE_MTS := 1;
                      else
                        :REQUIRE_MTS := 0;
                      end if;
                    elsif (sCHECK_SH_IN_HH_DEP = '2') then
                      if ((nAGES is not null and nAGES >= 18) and (nIN_RANGE_C00_D09 = 1 or nIN_RANGE_D45_D47 = 1)) then
                        :REQUIRE_MTS := 1;
                      else
                        :REQUIRE_MTS := 0;
                      end if;
                    else
                      :REQUIRE_MTS := 0;
                    end if;
                    :EXEC_MTS := 0;
                  end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_VIS_DIAGNOSISES_BASE;
          D_V_VISIT_CON_FIELDS;
          D_V_PERSMEDCARD_BASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS;
          D_V_AGENTS_BASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE;
          D_V_MKB10_BASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DIAGNS;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE;
      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_DAT_TOOLS.FULL_YEARS;
          D_PKG_MKB10.CHECK_CODE_IN_RANGE;

  [41] M2 DataSet: DS_DATETYPES
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              select u.CAPT,
                     u.ID
                from (select 'Назначить по: ' CAPT,
                             '0' ID
                        from dual
                      union
                      select 'Кол-во дней: ' CAPT,
                             '1' ID
                        from dual
                      union
                      select 'До выписки' CAPT,
                             '2' || '|' || (select to_char(hh.PLAN_DATE_OUT, 'dd.mm.yyyy')
                                              from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE hhd
                                                   join D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE hh on hh.ID = hhd.PID
                                             where hhd.ID = :HH_DEP) ID
                        from dual
                       where :HH_DEP is not null) u
               order by u.ID desc
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS_BASE;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORIES_BASE;

  [43] M2 DataSet: DS_MED_USE_METHODS
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
            @if (:CHECK_MULTI_USE == 1) {
              select dmu.ID,
                     dmu.MUM_NAME
                from D_V_MED_USE_METHODS dmu
               where dmu.ID in (select /*+ cardinality(t,1)*/ ids.COLUMN_VALUE
                                  from table(cast(D_PKG_TOOLS.STR_SEPARATE_TO_IDS((select t.MULTI_MED_USE_METHOD
                                                                                     from D_V_NOMMODIF_BASE t
                                                                                    where t.ID = :MULTI_USE)) as D_CL_ID)) ids)
            @} else {
              select t.ID,
                     t.MUM_NAME
                from D_V_MED_USE_METHODS t
               where t.version = D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU(1,:LPU,'MED_USE_METHODS')
                 and ((select count(1)
                         from D_V_MED_FORM_USE_METHODS
                        where pid = :MF) = 0
                      or exists (select null
                                   from D_V_MED_FORM_USE_METHODS mf
                                  where mf.PID = :MF
                                    and mf.USE_METHOD_ID = t.ID)
                     )
               order by MUM_NAME
            @}
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_MED_USE_METHODS;
          D_V_MED_FORM_USE_METHODS;
          D_V_NOMMODIF_BASE;
      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_VERSIONS.GET_VERSION_BY_LPU;
          D_PKG_TOOLS.STR_SEPARATE_TO_IDS;

  [44] M2 DataSet: DS_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  SELECT t.ID,
                         t.NOMMODIF_NAME,
                         t.EX_QUANTITY,
                         to_char(t.PLAN_DATE,'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi') PLAN_DATE1,
                         t.PLAN_DATE SORT_DATE,
                         TO_CHAR(mpp.NOMMODIF_DOSE*T.DOSE_QUANT,'FM9999999999999999990.009')||' '||T.DOSE_MEASURE DDOSE,
                         mpp.NOMMODIF_DOSE * t.DOSE_QUANT DOSES,
                         G.PART_SER
                    FROM D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS T
      				   join D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES mpp on mpp.ID = t.PID
                         left join D_V_GOODSSUPPLIES G on G.ID = T.GOODSUPPLY
                   WHERE t.LPU = :LPU
                     AND t.PID in (select v.COLUMN_VALUE
                                     from (select regexp_substr(:FULL_STR, '[^;]+', 1, level) COLUMN_VALUE
                                             from dual
                                          connect by level <= length(regexp_replace(:FULL_STR, '[^;]+')) + 1) v
                                  )
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES;
          D_V_GOODSSUPPLIES;

                  select nc.NOMMODIF_ID,
                         nc.NOMMODIF_NAME,

                         nd.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                         nd.DOSE_MEASURE_CODE                                                           DOSE_MES,
                         case when nd.ALT_MEASURE_CODE is not null and nd.KOEFF is not null then
                                replace(to_char(1 / nd.DOSE_PACK * nd.KOEFF, 'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',')
                              else
                                null
                         end                                                                            ALT_DOSE,

                         replace(to_char(1 / nd.DOSE_PACK, 'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',')        QUANTITY_DOSE,

                         0                                                                              RED_INJ

                                       and rownum = 1)
                union all

                         nd.DOSE                                                                            NOM_DOSE,

                         nd.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                         nd.DOSE_MEASURE_CODE                                                               DOSE_MES,
                         case when nd.ALT_MEASURE_CODE is not null and nd.KOEFF is not null then
                                replace(to_char(1 / nd.DOSE_PACK * nd.KOEFF, 'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',')
                              else
                                null
                         end                                                                                ALT_DOSE,
                         nd.ALT_MEASURE_CODE                                                                ALT_DOSE_MES,
                         replace(to_char(ps.DOSE_QUANT / nd.DOSE_PACK,'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',') QUANTITY_DOSE,
                         nd.MAIN_MEASURE_CODE                                                               QUANTITY_DOSE_MES,
                         nd.KOEFF,
                         nd.DOSE_PACK,
                         ps.DOSE_QUANT                                                                      COL_DOSE,
                         ps.RED_INJ
                    from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS ps

  [46] M2 DataSet: DS_EXTEMPO
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  select ps.NOMMODIF_ID,
                         nm.MOD_NAME NOMMODIF_NAME,
                         (ps.DOSE * ps.DOSE_QUANT) DOSE,
                         nm.DOSE NOM_DOSE,
                         'Дозировка:' || D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR(nm.DOSE) || ' ' || nm.DOSE_MEASURE_CODE DOSE_TEXT,
                         1 MP_CHECK,
                         replace(to_char(nm.DOSE,'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',') DOSE2,
                         nm.DOSE_MEASURE_ID,
                         nm.DOSE_MEASURE_CODE DOSE_MES,
                         case when nm.ALT_MEASURE_CODE is not null and nm.KOEFF is not null then
                                replace(to_char(ps.ALT_DOSE,'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',')
                         end ALT_DOSE,
                         nm.ALT_MEASURE_CODE ALT_DOSE_MES,
                         replace(to_char((ps.DOSE * ps.DOSE_QUANT) / nm.DOSE / nm.DOSE_PACK, 'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',') QUANTITY_DOSE,
                         nm.MAIN_MEASURE_CODE QUANTITY_DOSE_MES,
                         nm.KOEFF,
                         nm.DOSE_PACK,
                         ps.DOSE_QUANT COL_DOSE,
                         ps.RED_INJ
                    from (select ps.NOMMODIF_ID,
                                 ps.DOSE,
                                 ps.DOSE_QUANT,
                                 ps.QUANTITY,
                                 ps.ALT_DOSE,
                                 ps.RED_INJ
                            from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES p
                                 join D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS ps
                                   on ps.PID = p.ID
                                  and ps.NOMMODIF_ID != p.NOMMODIF_ID
                                  and ps.IS_EXTEMPO = 1
                           where p.ID = :ID
                        group by ps.NOMMODIF_ID,
                                 ps.DOSE,
                                 ps.DOSE_QUANT,
                                 ps.QUANTITY,
                                 ps.ALT_DOSE,
                                 ps.RED_INJ
                         ) ps
                         join D_V_NOMMODIF nm on nm.ID = ps.NOMMODIF_ID
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES;
          D_V_NOMMODIF;
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS;
      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_NUM_TOOLS.TO_STR;

  [47] M2 DataSet: DS_SCHEDULE
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
              select rownum MP_PRESCR_SPEC_ID,
                     mn.NOMMODIF_ID,
                     mn.SCH_TIME,
                     mn.DOSE_MEASURE SCHEDULE_DOSE_L,
                     mn.MAIN_MEASURE SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT_L,
                     replace(to_char(mn.DOSE,'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',') SCHEDULE_DOSE,
                     replace(to_char(mn.SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT, 'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',') SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT,
                     replace(to_char(mn.QUANTITY, 'FM99999999999999990.009'), '.', ',') SCHEDULE_DOSE_QU
                from (select distinct
                             mps.NOMMODIF_ID,
                           @if (:MP_CLASS == 4 || !empty(:MNN_ID)) {
                             mps.DOSE,
                             null SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT,
                           @} else {
                             mp.NOMMODIF_DOSE * mps.DOSE_QUANT DOSE,
                             case when nmd.ALT_MEASURE_ID is not null and nmd.KOEFF is not null
                                  then 1 / nmd.DOSE_PACK * nmd.KOEFF
                             end SCHEDULE_DOSE_ALT,
                           @}
                             mps.DOSE_QUANT QUANTITY,
                             to_char(mps.PLAN_DATE,'HH24:MI') SCH_TIME,
                             mps.DOSE_MEASURE,
                             mps.MAIN_MEASURE
                        from D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES mp
                             join D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS mps on mps.PID = mp.ID
                           @if(!((:MP_CLASS == 4 || !empty(:MNN_ID)))) {
                             join D_V_NOMMODIF_BASE nmd on nmd.ID = mps.NOMMODIF_ID
                           @}
                       where mp.ID = to_number(:ID)) mn
               order by mn.SCH_TIME
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBES;
          D_V_NOMMODIF_BASE;
          D_V_MP_PRESCRIBE_SPECS;

                     mf.MF_NAME
                from D_V_MED_FORMS mf

  [51] M2 Action: getDataForSchema
      Источник: /var/www/t-mis/mis/Forms/ArmPatientsInDep/SubForms/mp_prescribes_process_store.frm
      SQL:
      
                  begin
                    begin
                      select hhd.HOSP_DIAGN_TYPE_ID
                        into :MKB_TYPE
                        from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DIAGNS hhd
                       where hhd.HH_DEP = :HH_DEP
                         and hhd.HOSP_DIAGN_TYPE_ID in (0, 15, 16)
                         and rownum = 1
                         and hhd.LPU = :LPU
                       order by hhd.HOSP_DIAGN_TYPE_ID;
                    exception
                      when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                        :MKB_TYPE := null;
                    end;
      
                    begin
                      select case when coalesce(dr.DAYHOSPITAL_TYPE, to_char(dr.IS_DAY_HOSPITAL)) = 0 then 0 else 1 end
                        into :DAYHOSPITAL_TYPE
                        from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS hhd
                        join D_V_DEPS d
                          on d.ID = hhd.DEP_ID
                        join D_V_DEP_REQUISITES dr
                          on dr.PID = d.ID
                       where hhd.ID = :HH_DEP
                         and D_PKG_DAT_TOOLS.DATE_RANGES_ERROR(dr.DR_BGNDATE,
                                                               dr.DR_ENDDATE,
                                                               hhd.DATE_IN,
                                                               hhd.DATE_OUT,
                                                               1) > 0;
                    exception
                      when TOO_MANY_ROWS then
                        select case when coalesce(dr.DAYHOSPITAL_TYPE, to_char(dr.IS_DAY_HOSPITAL)) = 0 then 0 else 1 end
                          into :DAYHOSPITAL_TYPE
                          from D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS hhd
                          join D_V_DEPS d
                            on d.ID = hhd.DEP_ID
                          join D_V_DEP_REQUISITES dr
                            on dr.PID = d.ID
                         where hhd.ID = :HH_DEP
                           and dr.DR_ENDDATE is null;
                      when NO_DATA_FOUND then
                        :DAYHOSPITAL_TYPE := null;
                    end;
                  end;
              

      Таблицы/вьюхи:
          D_V_DEPS;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DEPS;
          D_V_HOSP_HISTORY_DIAGNS;
          D_V_DEP_REQUISITES;
      Пакеты/функции:
          D_PKG_DAT_TOOLS.DATE_RANGES_ERROR;
